 </small>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row" style="padding:0px 2px;white-space:nowrap">\n         Areas affected\n        </th>\n        <td style="padding:0px 2px">\n         <a href="/wiki/Windward_Islands" title="Windward Islands">\n          Windward Islands\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <a href="/wiki/Suriname" title="Suriname">\n          Suriname\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <a href="/wiki/Guyana" title="Guyana">\n          Guyana\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <a href="/wiki/Nicaragua" title="Nicaragua">\n          Nicaragua\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <a href="/wiki/Honduras" title="Honduras">\n          Honduras\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <a href="/wiki/Belize" title="Belize">\n          Belize\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <a href="/wiki/Cayman_Islands" title="Cayman Islands">\n          Cayman Islands\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <a href="/wiki/Yucat%C3%A1n_Peninsula" title="Yucat\xc3\xa1n <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;padding:0px 2px">\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center; border-top:#aaa 1px solid;">\n         Part of the\n         <b>\n          <a href="/wiki/2017_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2017 Atlantic hurricane season">\n           2017 Atlantic hurricane season\n          </a>\n         </b>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr style="display:none">\n        <td colspan="2">\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       <b>\n        Hurricane Harvey\n       </b>\n       was the costliest\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone" title="Tropical cyclone">\n        tropical cyclone\n       </a>\n       on record, surpassing the record set by\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Katrina" title="Hurricane Katrina">\n        Hurricane Katrina\n       </a>\n       , and is the second-costliest natural disaster worldwide, behind only the\n       <a href="/wiki/2011_T%C5%8Dhoku_earthquake_and_tsunami" title="2011 T\xc5\x8dhoku earthquake and tsunami">\n        2011 Japan earthquake and tsunami\n       </a>\n       . It was the first\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/SSHS#Category_3" title="SSHS">\n        major hurricane\n       </a>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-1">\n         [nb 1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       to make\n       <a href="/wiki/Landfall" title="Landfall">\n        landfall\n       </a>\n       in the\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">\n        United States\n       </a>\n       since\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Wilma" title="Hurricane Wilma">\n        Wilma\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/2005_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2005 Atlantic hurricane season">\n        2005\n       </a>\n       , ending a record 12-year span in which no hurricanes made landfall at such an intensity in the country. In a four-day period, many areas received more than 40 inches (100\xc2\xa0cm) of rain as the system slowly meandered over eastern Texas and adjacent waters, causing catastrophic flooding. With peak accumulations of 64.58\xc2\xa0in (164.0\xc2\xa0cm), Harvey was the\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_wettest_tropical_cyclones_in_the_United_States" title="List of wettest tropical cyclones in the United States">\n        wettest tropical cyclone on record in the United States\n       </a>\n       . The resulting floods inundated hundreds of thousands of homes, displaced more than 30,000\xc2\xa0people, and prompted more than 17,000\xc2\xa0rescues. A\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_Category_4_Atlantic_hurricanes" title="List of Category 4 Atlantic hurricanes">\n        Category\xc2\xa04 hurricane\n       </a>\n       at its peak intensity, it was the strongest and most intense hurricane in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Gulf_of_Mexico" title="Gulf of Mexico">\n        Gulf of Mexico\n       </a>\n       since\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Rita" title="Hurricane Rita">\n        Rita\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/2005_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2005 Atlantic hurricane season">\n        2005\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The eighth\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone_naming" title="Tropical cyclone naming">\n        named storm\n       </a>\n       , third\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricane" title="Hurricane">\n        hurricane\n       </a>\n       , and the first major hurricane of the extremely active\n       <a href="/wiki/2017_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2017 Atlantic hurricane season">\n        2017 Atlantic hurricane season\n       </a>\n       , Harvey developed from a\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_wave" title="Tropical wave">\n        tropical wave\n       </a>\n       to the east of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Lesser_Antilles" title="Lesser Antilles">\n        Lesser Antilles\n       </a>\n       , reaching\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tropical_storm" title="Tropical storm">\n        tropical storm\n       </a>\n       status on August\xc2\xa017. The storm crossed through the\n       <a href="/wiki/Windward_Islands" title="Windward Islands">\n        Windward Islands\n       </a>\n       on the following day, passing just south of\n       <a href="/wiki/Barbados" title="Barbados">\n        Barbados\n       </a>\n       and later near\n       <a href="/wiki/Saint_Vincent_(Antilles)" title="Saint Vincent (Antilles)">\n        Saint Vincent\n       </a>\n       . Upon entering the\n       <a href="/wiki/Caribbean_Sea" title="Caribbean Sea">\n        Caribbean Sea\n       </a>\n       , Harvey began to weaken due to moderate\n       <a href="/wiki/Wind_shear" title="Wind shear">\n        wind shear\n       </a>\n       and degenerated into a tropical wave north of\n       <a href="/wiki/Colombia" title="Colombia">\n        Colombia\n       </a>\n       early on August\xc2\xa019. The remnants were monitored for regeneration as it continued west-northwestward across the Caribbean and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Yucat%C3%A1n_Peninsula" title="Yucat\xc3\xa1n Peninsula">\n        Yucat\xc3\xa1n Peninsula\n       </a>\n       , before redeveloping over the\n       <a href="/wiki/Bay_of_Campeche" title="Bay of Campeche">\n        Bay of Campeche\n       </a>\n       on August\xc2\xa023. Harvey then began to rapidly intensify on August\xc2\xa024, regaining tropical storm status and becoming a hurricane later that day. While the storm moved generally northwest, Harvey\'s intensification phase stalled slightly overnight from August\xc2\xa024\xe2\x80\x9325; however, Harvey soon resumed strengthening and quickly became a major hurricane and attained Category\xc2\xa04 intensity later that day. Hours later, Harvey made landfall near\n       <a href="/wiki/Rockport,_Texas" title="Rockport, Texas">\n        Rockport, Texas\n       </a>\n       , at peak intensity. Afterwards, rapid weakening ensued, and Harvey had downgraded to a tropical storm as it stalled near the coastline of the state, dropping torrential and unprecedented amounts of rainfall over the Lone Star state. On August\xc2\xa028, it emerged back over the Gulf of Mexico, strengthening slightly before making a third and final landfall in\n       <a href="/wiki/Louisiana" title="Louisiana">\n        Louisiana\n       </a>\n       on August\xc2\xa029. As Harvey drifted inland, it quickly weakened again as it became extratropical on September\xc2\xa01, before dissipating two days later.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Harvey caused at least 91 confirmed deaths: 1 in\n       <a href="/wiki/Guyana" title="Guyana">\n        Guyana\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cdema_2-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-cdema-2">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and 90 in the United States.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Harvey_and_Irma_3-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Harvey_and_Irma-3">\n         [2]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Xinhua_Net_death_toll_4-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Xinhua_Net_death_toll-4">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Chron_death_toll_5-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Chron_death_toll-5">\n         [4]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-The_Birmingham_News_6-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-The_Birmingham_News-6">\n         [5]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7">\n        <a href="#cite_note-7">\n         [6]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-just_died_8-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-just_died-8">\n         [7]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Total damage from the hurricane is estimated at $198.63\xc2\xa0billion, making it the costliest natural disaster ever in the United States.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-198billion_9-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-198billion-9">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="toclimit-3">\n       <div class="toc" id="toc">\n        <div class="toctitle">\n         <h2>\n          Contents\n         </h2>\n        </div>\n        <ul>\n         <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-1">\n          <a href="#Meteorological_history">\n           <span class="tocnumber">\n            1\n           </span>\n           <span class="toctext">\n            Meteorological history\n           </span>\n          </a>\n          <ul>\n           <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-2">\n            <a href="#Formation_and_initial_degeneration_.28Caribbean.29">\n             <span class="tocnumber">\n              1.1\n             </span>\n             <span class="toctext">\n              Formation and initial degeneration (Caribbean)\n             </span>\n            </a>\n           </li>\n           <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-3">\n            <a href="#Regeneration.2C_peak_intensity.2C_and_stalling_.28Gulf_of_Mexico.29">\n             <span class="tocnumber">\n              1.2\n             </span>\n             <span class="toctext">\n              Regeneration, peak intensity, and stalling (Gulf of Mexico)\n             </span>\n            </a>\n           </li>\n           <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-4">\n            <a href="#Final_landfall_and_dissipation_.28Eastern_United_States.29">\n             <span class="tocnumber">\n              1.3\n             </span>\n             <span class="toctext">\n              Final landfall and dissipation (Eastern United States)\n             </span>\n            </a>\n           </li>\n          </ul>\n         </li>\n         <li class="toclevel-1 </span>\n          </a>\n          <ul>\n           <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-6">\n            <a href="#Caribbean_and_Latin_America">\n             <span class="tocnumber">\n              2.1\n             </span>\n             <span class="toctext">\n              Caribbean and Latin America\n             </span>\n            </a>\n           </li>\n           <li class="toclevel-2 States\n             </span>\n            </a>\n            <ul>\n             <li class="toclevel-3 tocsection-8">\n              <a href="#Video_briefings_by_officials">\n               <span class="tocnumber">\n                2.2.1\n               </span>\n               <span class="toctext">\n                Video briefings by officials\n               </span>\n              </a>\n             </li>\n             <li class="toclevel-3 tocsection-9">\n              <a href="#Texas">\n               <span class="tocnumber">\n                2.2.2\n               </span>\n               <span class="toctext">\n                Texas\n               </span>\n              </a>\n             </li>\n             <li class="toclevel-3 tocsection-10">\n              <a href="#Louisiana">\n               <span class="tocnumber">\n                2.2.3\n               </span>\n               <span class="toctext">\n                Louisiana\n               </span>\n              </a>\n             </li>\n            </ul>\n           </li>\n          </ul>\n         </li>\n         <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-11">\n          <a Latin America\n           </span>\n          </a>\n         </li>\n         <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-12">\n          <a href="#Effects_in_the_United_States">\n           <span class="tocnumber">\n            4\n           </span>\n           <span class="toctext">\n            Effects in the United States\n           </span>\n          </a>\n          <ul>\n           <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-13">\n            <a href="#Texas_2">\n             <span class="tocnumber">\n              4.1\n             </span>\n             <span class="toctext">\n              Texas\n             </span>\n            </a>\n            <ul>\n             <li class="toclevel-3 tocsection-14">\n              <a href="#Landfall_area">\n               <span class="tocnumber">\n                4.1.1\n               </span>\n               <span class="toctext">\n                Landfall area\n               </span>\n              </a>\n             </li>\n             <li class="toclevel-3 tocsection-15">\n              <a href="#Houston_metropolitan_area_flooding">\n               <span class="tocnumber">\n                4.1.2\n               </span>\n               <span class="toctext">\n                Houston metropolitan area flooding\n               </span>\n              </a>\n             </li>\n             <li class="toclevel-3 tocsection-16">\n              <a href="#Deep_East_Texas_and_Beaumont.E2.80.93Port_Arthur_area">\n               <span class="tocnumber">\n                4.1.3\n               </span>\n               <span class="toctext">\n                Deep East Texas and Beaumont\xe2\x80\x93Port Arthur area\n               </span>\n              </a>\n             </li>\n            </ul>\n           </li>\n           <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-17">\n            <a href="#Louisiana_2">\n             <span class="tocnumber">\n              4.2\n             </span>\n             <span class="toctext">\n              Louisiana\n             </span>\n            </a>\n           </li>\n           <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-18">\n            <a href="#Elsewhere">\n             <span class="tocnumber">\n              4.3\n             </span>\n             <span class="toctext">\n              Elsewhere\n             </span>\n            </a>\n           </li>\n           <li class="toclevel-2 production\n             </span>\n            </a>\n           </li>\n           <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-20">\n            <a href="#Sports">\n             <span class="tocnumber">\n              4.5\n             </span>\n             <span class="toctext">\n              Sports\n             </span>\n            </a>\n           </li>\n          </ul>\n         </li>\n         <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-21">\n          <a href="#Aftermath">\n           <span class="tocnumber">\n            5\n           </span>\n           <span class="toctext">\n            Aftermath\n           </span>\n          </a>\n          <ul>\n           <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-22">\n            <a href="#Texas_3">\n             <span class="tocnumber">\n              5.1\n             </span>\n             <span class="toctext">\n              Texas\n             </span>\n            </a>\n           </li>\n           <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-23">\n            <a href="#Economic_loss_estimates">\n             <span class="tocnumber">\n              5.2\n             </span>\n             <span class="toctext">\n              Economic loss estimates\n             </span>\n            </a>\n           </li>\n           <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-24">\n            <a href="#Federal_government_response">\n             <span class="tocnumber">\n              5.3\n             </span>\n             <span class="toctext">\n              Federal government response\n             </span>\n            </a>\n           </li>\n           <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-25">\n            <a href="#Non-governmental_organization_response">\n             <span class="tocnumber">\n              5.4\n             </span>\n             <span class="toctext">\n              Non-governmental organization response\n             </span>\n            </a>\n           </li>\n           <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-26">\n            <a href="#Foreign_government_response">\n             <span class="tocnumber">\n              5.5\n             </span>\n             <span class="toctext">\n              Foreign government response\n             </span>\n            </a>\n           </li>\n           <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-27">\n            <a href="#Health_and_environmental_hazards_in_flood_waters">\n             <span class="tocnumber">\n              5.6\n             </span>\n             <span class="toctext">\n              Health and environmental hazards in flood waters\n             </span>\n            </a>\n           </li>\n          </ul>\n         </li>\n         <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-28">\n          <a href="#Environmental_factors">\n           <span class="tocnumber">\n            6\n           </span>\n           <span class="toctext">\n            Environmental factors\n           </span>\n          </a>\n          <ul>\n           <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-29">\n            <a href="#Urban_development">\n             <span class="tocnumber">\n              6.1\n             </span>\n             <span class="toctext">\n              Urban development\n             </span>\n            </a>\n           </li>\n           <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-30">\n            <a href="#Subsidence">\n             <span class="tocnumber">\n              6.2\n             </span>\n             <span class="toctext">\n              Subsidence\n             </span>\n            </a>\n           </li>\n           <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-31">\n            <a href="#Climate_change">\n             <span class="tocnumber">\n              6.3\n             </span>\n             <span class="toctext">\n              Climate change\n             </span>\n            </a>\n           </li>\n          </ul>\n         </li>\n         <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-32">\n          <a href="#See_also">\n           <span class="tocnumber">\n            7\n           </span>\n           <span class="toctext">\n            See also\n           </span>\n          </a>\n         </li>\n         <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-33">\n          <a href="#Notes">\n           <span class="tocnumber">\n            8\n           </span>\n           <span class="toctext">\n            Notes\n           </span>\n          </a>\n         </li>\n         <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-34">\n          <a href="#References">\n           <span class="tocnumber">\n            9\n           </span>\n           <span class="toctext">\n            References\n           </span>\n          </a>\n         </li>\n         <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-35">\n          <a href="#External_links">\n           <span class="tocnumber">\n            10\n           </span>\n           <span class="toctext">\n            External links\n           </span>\n          </a>\n         </li>\n        </ul>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Meteorological_history">\n        Meteorological history\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Harvey&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Meteorological history">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Harvey_2017_track.png">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1854" data-file-width="3000" height="185" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Harvey_2017_track.png/300px-Harvey_2017_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Harvey_2017_track.png/450px-Harvey_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Harvey_2017_track.png/600px-Harvey_2017_track.png 2x" width="300"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Harvey_2017_track.png" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Map plotting the track and intensity of the storm according to the\n         <a href="/wiki/Saffir%E2%80%93Simpson_scale" title="Saffir\xe2\x80\x93Simpson scale">\n          Saffir\xe2\x80\x93Simpson scale\n         </a>\n         .\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="Formation_and_initial_degeneration_(Caribbean)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Formation_and_initial_degeneration_.28Caribbean.29">\n        Formation and initial degeneration (Caribbean)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Harvey&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Formation and initial degeneration (Caribbean)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Early on August\xc2\xa013, the\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Hurricane_Center" title="National Hurricane Center">\n        National Hurricane Center\n       </a>\n       (NHC) began monitoring a\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_wave" title="Tropical wave">\n        tropical wave\n       </a>\n       on the western coast of Africa. Amid favorable environmental conditions, the wave was expected to merge with a broad\n       <a href="/wiki/Low-pressure_area" title="Low-pressure area">\n        area of low pressure\n       </a>\n       to its east southwest of\n       <a href="/wiki/Cape_Verde" title="Cape Verde">\n        Cape Verde\n       </a>\n       and gradually organize thereafter.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10">\n        <a href="#cite_note-10">\n         [9]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Instead, the two disturbances remained separate, with the broad trough continuing westward and the tropical wave moving farther north, eventually becoming\n       <a href="/wiki/2017_Atlantic_hurricane_season#Other_systems" title="2017 Atlantic hurricane season">\n        Potential Tropical Cyclone Ten\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11">\n        <a href="#cite_note-11">\n         [10]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On August\xc2\xa017, shower and thunderstorm activity in association with the trough began to show signs of organization,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12">\n        <a href="#cite_note-12">\n         [11]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       while high-resolution satellite showed an increasingly defined low-level circulation.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13">\n        <a href="#cite_note-13">\n         [12]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As such, the NHC initiated advisories on a potential tropical cyclone, allowing tropical storm watches and warnings to be hoisted for portions of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Lesser_Antilles" title="Lesser Antilles">\n        Lesser Antilles\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Beven_14-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Beven-14">\n         [13]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       An\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_hunters" title="Hurricane hunters">\n        Air Force Reserve Hurricane Hunter aircraft\n       </a>\n       deployed to the disturbance later that afternoon found a well-defined center and tropical storm-force winds, prompting the NHC to upgrade it to Tropical Storm Harvey at 21:00\xc2\xa0UTC.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Disc2_15-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Disc2-15">\n         [14]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Following its designation, the cyclone moved swiftly westward into the\n       <a href="/wiki/Caribbean_Sea" title="Caribbean Sea">\n        Caribbean Sea\n       </a>\n       under the influence of an expansive\n       <a href="/wiki/High-pressure_area" title="High-pressure area">\n        ridge of high pressure\n       </a>\n       to its north. An environment of moderate\n       <a href="/wiki/Wind_shear" title="Wind shear">\n        wind shear\n       </a>\n       complicated the weather of the storm\'s intensity, with global forecast models suggesting dissipation in the central Caribbean, whereas statistical and hurricane models suggested the potential for Harvey to be near hurricane strength in later days.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Disc2_15-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Disc2-15">\n         [14]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Over the next day, the storm changed little in structure, remaining poorly organized with its low-level center on the eastern edge of associated deep\n       <a href="/wiki/Convection" title="Convection">\n        convection\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16">\n        <a href="#cite_note-16">\n         [15]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Harvey\'s presentation began to deteriorate early on August\xc2\xa019; its convective pattern became elongated while the circulation became less defined. In fact, a reconnaissance aircraft was unable to find a loosely-closed circulation at 850\xc2\xa0mb (4,781\xc2\xa0ft), though it did locate one at lower levels.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17">\n        <a href="#cite_note-17">\n         [16]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Harvey was downgraded to a tropical depression at 21:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August\xc2\xa019;\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18">\n        <a href="#cite_note-18">\n         [17]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       six hours later, based on continued data from a\n       <a href="/wiki/Reconnaissance_aircraft" title="Reconnaissance aircraft">\n        reconnaissance aircraft\n       </a>\n       , it was declared an open\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_wave" title="Tropical wave">\n        tropical wave\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-19">\n        <a href="#cite_note-19">\n         [18]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Harvey_during_the_eclipse.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="5053" data-file-width="6052" height="184" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/68/Harvey_during_the_eclipse.jpg/220px-Harvey_during_the_eclipse.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/68/Harvey_during_the_eclipse.jpg/330px-Harvey_during_the_eclipse.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/68/Harvey_during_the_eclipse.jpg/440px-Harvey_during_the_eclipse.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Harvey_during_the_eclipse.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         The remnants of Harvey as a tropical wave, over the\n         <a href="/wiki/Gulf_of_Honduras" title="Gulf of Honduras">\n          Gulf of Honduras\n         </a>\n         on August 21, within the shadow of\n         <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse_of_August_21,_2017" title="Solar eclipse of August 21, 2017">\n          a total solar eclipse\n         </a>\n         .\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Early on August\xc2\xa020, the NHC began monitoring the remnants of Harvey for redevelopment. Although the effects of strong upper-level winds and dry air were expected to limit development in the near-term, conditions were expected to become more conducive to tropical storm and hurricane conditions when the disturbance entered the northwestern Caribbean Sea, and especially in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Bay_of_Campeche" title="Bay of Campeche">\n        Bay of Campeche\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20">\n        <a href="#cite_note-20">\n         [19]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Despite an increase in convective organization, the disturbance still lacked a well-defined center as it approached the\n       <a href="/wiki/Yucat%C3%A1n_Peninsula" title="Yucat\xc3\xa1n Peninsula">\n        Yucat\xc3\xa1n Peninsula\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21">\n        <a href="#cite_note-21">\n         [20]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       While traversing inland, satellite images and surface observations indicated that the circulation became better defined.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-22">\n        <a href="#cite_note-22">\n         [21]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="Regeneration,_peak_intensity,_and_stalling_(Gulf_of_Mexico)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Regeneration.2C_peak_intensity.2C_and_stalling_.28Gulf_of_Mexico.29">\n        Regeneration, peak intensity, and stalling (Gulf of Mexico)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Harvey&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Regeneration, peak intensity, and stalling (Gulf of Mexico)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       A reconnaissance aircraft investigating the remnants of Harvey around 15:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August\xc2\xa023 indicated that it once again acquired a well-defined center, and the NHC upgraded it to a tropical depression accordingly.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23">\n        <a href="#cite_note-23">\n         [22]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The system began to slowly consolidate amid an increasingly favorable environment,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-24">\n        <a href="#cite_note-24">\n         [23]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       attaining tropical storm intensity by 06:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August\xc2\xa024.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-25">\n        <a href="#cite_note-25">\n         [24]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Later that morning, Harvey began to undergo\n       <a href="/wiki/Rapid_intensification" title="Rapid intensification">\n        rapid intensification\n       </a>\n       as an\n       <a href="/wiki/Eye_(cyclone)" title="Eye (cyclone)">\n        eye\n       </a>\n       developed and its\n       <a href="/wiki/Atmospheric_pressure" title="Atmospheric pressure">\n        central pressure\n       </a>\n       quickly fell.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-26">\n        <a href="#cite_note-26">\n         [25]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       By 17:00\xc2\xa0UTC, the storm was upgraded to the third hurricane of the season.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27">\n        <a href="#cite_note-27">\n         [26]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Slight entrainment of dry air slowed the intensification process, however, by the next day, Harvey was able to quickly strengthen into a Category\xc2\xa03 major hurricane by 19:00\xc2\xa0UTC.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-28">\n        <a href="#cite_note-28">\n         [27]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Further deepening occurred as the storm approached the coast of Texas, with Harvey becoming a Category\xc2\xa04 hurricane at 23:00\xc2\xa0UTC, based on reconnaissance aircraft data.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-29">\n        <a href="#cite_note-29">\n         [28]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Around 03:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August\xc2\xa026, the hurricane made landfall at peak intensity at\n       <a href="/wiki/Rockport,_Texas" title="Rockport, Texas">\n        Rockport\n       </a>\n       with winds of 130\xc2\xa0mph (215\xc2\xa0km/h) and an\n       <a href="/wiki/Atmospheric_pressure" title="Atmospheric pressure">\n        atmospheric pressure\n       </a>\n       of 938\n       <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n        mbar\n       </a>\n       (27.7\n       <a href="/wiki/Inch_of_mercury" title="Inch of mercury">\n        inHg\n       </a>\n       ).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-30">\n        <a href="#cite_note-30">\n         [29]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Harvey became the first major hurricane to make landfall in the United States since\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Wilma" title="Hurricane Wilma">\n        Wilma\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/2005_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2005 Atlantic hurricane season">\n        2005\n       </a>\n       and the strongest in terms of wind speed to hit the country since\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Charley" title="Hurricane Charley">\n        Charley\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/2004_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2004 Atlantic hurricane season">\n        2004\n       </a>\n       . It was the first hurricane to strike Texas since\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Ike" title="Hurricane Ike">\n        Hurricane Ike\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/2008_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2008 Atlantic hurricane season">\n        2008\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-31">\n        <a href="#cite_note-31">\n         [30]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       the first major hurricane in the state since\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricane_Bret_(1999)" title="Hurricane Bret (1999)">\n        Bret\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/1999_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="1999 Atlantic hurricane season">\n        1999\n       </a>\n       , and the strongest in Texas since\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Carla" title="Hurricane Carla">\n        Carla\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/1961_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="1961 Atlantic hurricane season">\n        1961\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-32">\n        <a href="#cite_note-32">\n         [31]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:As_expected_Harvey_has_intensified_into_a_Hurricane_(35973025253).jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1080" data-file-width="1920" height="169" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e8/As_expected_Harvey_has_intensified_into_a_Hurricane_%2835973025253%29.jpg/300px-As_expected_Harvey_has_intensified_into_a_Hurricane_%2835973025253%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e8/As_expected_Harvey_has_intensified_into_a_Hurricane_%2835973025253%29.jpg/450px-As_expected_Harvey_has_intensified_into_a_Hurricane_%2835973025253%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e8/As_expected_Harvey_has_intensified_into_a_Hurricane_%2835973025253%29.jpg/600px-As_expected_Harvey_has_intensified_into_a_Hurricane_%2835973025253%29.jpg 2x" width="300"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:As_expected_Harvey_has_intensified_into_a_Hurricane_(35973025253).jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Harvey as a hurricane on August\xc2\xa024\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       After striking land, the storm moved over the\n       <a href="/wiki/Copano_Bay" title="Copano Bay">\n        Copano Bay\n       </a>\n       and made a second landfall in Texas just north of\n       <a href="/wiki/Holiday_Beach,_Texas" title="Holiday Beach, Texas">\n        Holiday Beach\n       </a>\n       at 06:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August\xc2\xa026 as a Category\xc2\xa03 hurricane.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33">\n        <a href="#cite_note-33">\n         [32]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Afterwards, rapid weakening ensued as its speed slowed dramatically to a crawl, and Harvey weakened to a tropical storm at 18:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August\xc2\xa026.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-34">\n        <a href="#cite_note-34">\n         [33]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       For about two days the storm stalled just inland, dropping very heavy rainfall and causing widespread flash flooding. Harvey\'s center drifted back towards the southeast, positioning itself near or just off the Texas coast at\n       <a href="/wiki/Matagorda,_Texas" title="Matagorda, Texas">\n        Matagorda\n       </a>\n       by 15:00 UTC on August 28.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-35">\n        <a href="#cite_note-35">\n         [34]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Once offshore, convection blossomed and allowed the once-exposed low-level circulation to become obscured. An Air Force reconnaissance plane investigating the system during the afternoon of August\xc2\xa029 found that maximum winds had increased to 50\xc2\xa0mph (85\xc2\xa0km/h).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-36">\n        <a href="#cite_note-36">\n         [35]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Around 09:00\xc2\xa0UTC the next morning, Harvey made its third and final landfall just west of\n       <a href="/wiki/Cameron,_Louisiana" title="Cameron, Louisiana">\n        Cameron, Louisiana\n       </a>\n       , with winds of 45\xc2\xa0mph (75\xc2\xa0km/h).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-37">\n        <a href="#cite_note-37">\n         [36]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="Final_landfall_and_dissipation_(Eastern_United_States)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Final_landfall_and_dissipation_.28Eastern_United_States.29">\n        Final landfall and dissipation (Eastern United States)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Harvey&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Final landfall and dissipation (Eastern United States)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The system continued north and then north-northeast, weakening to a tropical depression over central Louisiana around 00:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August\xc2\xa030.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-38">\n        <a href="#cite_note-38">\n         [37]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Associated convection with Harvey became focused north of the center and along a warm front on September\xc2\xa01, indicating that the system transitioned into a post-tropical cyclone by 15:00\xc2\xa0UTC that day.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-39">\n        <a href="#cite_note-39">\n         [38]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       However, Harvey\'s remnants continued moving northeastward, while slowly weakening. Late on September 2, the WPC issued its final advisory on Harvey\'s remnant low, while it was located over\n       <a href="/wiki/Ohio" title="Ohio">\n        Ohio\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-final_WPC_advisory_40-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-final_WPC_advisory-40">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Harvey\'s remnants continued to drift northward, before being absorbed by another low pressure system north of\n       <a href="/wiki/Lake_Erie" title="Lake Erie">\n        Lake Erie\n       </a>\n       , late on September 3.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WPC_weather_map_on_Sep_3_41-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-WPC_weather_map_on_Sep_3-41">\n         [40]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Preparations">\n        Preparations\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Harvey&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Preparations">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Caribbean_and_Latin_America">\n        Caribbean and Latin America\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Harvey&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Caribbean and Latin America">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Harvey_2017-08-18_Suomi_NPP.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2869" data-file-width="2048" height="308" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6e/Harvey_2017-08-18_Suomi_NPP.jpg/220px-Harvey_2017-08-18_Suomi_NPP.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6e/Harvey_2017-08-18_Suomi_NPP.jpg/330px-Harvey_2017-08-18_Suomi_NPP.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6e/Harvey_2017-08-18_Suomi_NPP.jpg/440px-Harvey_2017-08-18_Suomi_NPP.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Harvey_2017-08-18_Suomi_NPP.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Tropical Storm Harvey in the Eastern Caribbean on August 18\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone_warnings_and_watches" title="Tropical cyclone warnings and watches">\n        Tropical cyclone warnings and watches\n       </a>\n       for the\n       <a href="/wiki/Windward_Islands" title="Windward Islands">\n        Windward Islands\n       </a>\n       were issued starting at 15:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August\xc2\xa017, about six hours before Harvey developed. At that time, a tropical storm watch was posted for\n       <a href="/wiki/Dominica" title="Dominica">\n        Dominica\n       </a>\n       , while a tropical storm warning became in effect in\n       <a href="/wiki/Barbados" title="Barbados">\n        Barbados\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Martinique" title="Martinique">\n        Martinique\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Saint_Lucia" title="Saint Lucia">\n        Saint Lucia\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Saint_Vincent_and_the_Grenadines" title="Saint Vincent and the Grenadines">\n        Saint Vincent and the Grenadines\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Beven_14-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Beven-14">\n         [13]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       All watches and warnings were discontinued by late on August\xc2\xa018, as the storm continued westward into the Caribbean.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42">\n        <a href="#cite_note-42">\n         [41]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In Honduras, a green alert was issued for the\n       <a href="/wiki/Atl%C3%A1ntida_Department" title="Atl\xc3\xa1ntida Department">\n        Atl\xc3\xa1ntida\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Bay_Islands_Department" title="Bay Islands Department">\n        Islas de la Bah\xc3\xada\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Col%C3%B3n_Department_(Honduras)" title="Col\xc3\xb3n Department (Honduras)">\n        Col\xc3\xb3n\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Cort%C3%A9s_Department" title="Cort\xc3\xa9s Department">\n        Cort\xc3\xa9s\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Gracias_a_Dios_Department" title="Gracias a Dios Department">\n        Gracias a Dios\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Olancho_Department" title="Olancho Department">\n        Olancho\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Yoro_Department" title="Yoro Department">\n        Yoro\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Departments_of_Honduras" title="Departments of Honduras">\n        departments\n       </a>\n       . About 8 inches (20\xc2\xa0cm) of precipitation was expected along the coast, while inland areas were forecast to receive 2.76 to 3.15\xc2\xa0in (7.0 to 8.0\xc2\xa0cm) of rain.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-43">\n        <a href="#cite_note-43">\n         [42]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As the remnants of Harvey approached Mexico, the Civil Protection Secretary of the state of\n       <a href="/wiki/Campeche" title="Campeche">\n        Campeche\n       </a>\n       issued a blue alert, indicting minimal danger.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-44">\n        <a href="#cite_note-44">\n         [43]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       When Harvey redeveloped at 15:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August\xc2\xa023, the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Government_of_Mexico" title="Government of Mexico">\n        Government of Mexico\n       </a>\n       issued a tropical storm watch in\n       <a href="/wiki/Tamaulipas" title="Tamaulipas">\n        Tamaulipas\n       </a>\n       from Boca De Catan to the mouth of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Rio_Grande" title="Rio Grande">\n        Rio Grande\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ad12_45-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ad12-45">\n         [44]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The watch remained in effect until 21:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August\xc2\xa025, after it became evident that the storm no longer posed a significant threat to that area.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ad22_46-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ad22-46">\n         [45]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="United_States">\n        United States\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Harvey&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: United States">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       FEMA worked with the\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Coast_Guard" title="United States Coast Guard">\n        Coast Guard\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/U.S._Customs_and_Border_Protection" title="U.S. Customs and Border Protection">\n        Customs and Border Protection\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/U.S._Immigration_and_Customs_Enforcement" title="U.S. Immigration and Customs Enforcement">\n        Immigration and Customs Enforcement\n       </a>\n       to prepare for the storm and its aftermath. The agency placed disaster response teams on standby at emergency posts in\n       <a href="/wiki/Austin,_Texas" title="Austin, Texas">\n        Austin, Texas\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Baton_Rouge,_Louisiana" title="Baton Rouge, Louisiana">\n        Baton Rouge, Louisiana\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-47">\n        <a href="#cite_note-47">\n         [46]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Video_briefings_by_officials">\n        Video briefings by officials\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-traditional">\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           Comments from National Weather Service director\n           <a class="new"       </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div </a>\n           </div>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           Comments by the\n           <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_Texas" title="Governor of Texas">\n            Governor of Texas\n           </a>\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Texas">\n        Texas\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Harvey&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Texas">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       Upon the NHC resuming advisories for Harvey at 15:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August\xc2\xa023, a hurricane watch was issued in\n       <a href="/wiki/Texas" title="Texas">\n        Texas\n       </a>\n       from\n       <a href="/wiki/Port_Mansfield,_Texas" title="Port Mansfield, Texas">\n        Port Mansfield\n       </a>\n       to\n       <a href="/wiki/San_Luis_Pass" title="San Luis Pass">\n        San Luis Pass\n       </a>\n       , while a tropical storm watch was posted from Port Mansfield south to the mouth of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Rio_Grande" title="Rio Grande">\n        Rio Grande\n       </a>\n       and from San Luis Pass to\n       <a href="/wiki/High_Island,_Texas" title="High Island, Texas">\n        High Island\n       </a>\n       . Additionally, a storm surge watch became in effect from Port Mansfield to High Island.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ad12_45-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ad12-45">\n         [44]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Additional watches and warnings were posted in these areas at 09:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August\xc2\xa024, with a hurricane warning from Port Mansfield to\n       <a href="/wiki/Matagorda,_Texas" title="Matagorda, Texas">\n        Matagorda\n       </a>\n       ; a tropical storm warning from Matagorda to High Island; a hurricane watch and tropical storm warning from Port Mansfield to the Rio Grande; a storm surge warning from Port Mansfield to San Luis Pass; and a storm surge from Port Mansfield to the Rio Grande.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-48">\n        <a href="#cite_note-48">\n         [47]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The watches and warnings were adjusted accordingly after Harvey moved inland and began weakening, with the warning discontinued at 15:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August\xc2\xa026.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-49">\n        <a href="#cite_note-49">\n         [48]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       By 09:00\xc2\xa0UTC on the following day, only a tropical storm warning and a storm surge warning remained in effect from\n       <a href="/wiki/Port_O%27Connor,_Texas" title="Port O\'Connor, Texas">\n        Port O\'Connor\n       </a>\n       to\n       <a href="/wiki/Sargent,_Texas" title="Sargent, Texas">\n        Sargent\n       </a>\n       . However, watches and warnings were re-issued as Harvey began to re-emerge into the Gulf of Mexico, and beginning at 15:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August\xc2\xa028, a tropical storm warning was in effect for the entire Gulf Coast of Texas from High Island northward.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ad33_50-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ad33-50">\n         [49]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Governor\n       <a href="/wiki/Greg_Abbott" title="Greg Abbott">\n        Greg Abbott\n       </a>\n       declared a\n       <a href="/wiki/State_of_emergency" title="State of emergency">\n        state of emergency\n       </a>\n       for 30\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_counties_in_Texas" title="List of counties in Texas">\n        counties\n       </a>\n       on August\xc2\xa023, while mandatory evacuations were issued for\n       <a href="/wiki/Brazoria_County,_Texas" title="Brazoria County, Texas">\n        Brazoria\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Calhoun_County,_Texas" title="Calhoun County, Texas">\n        Calhoun\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Jackson_County,_Texas" title="Jackson County, Texas">\n        Jackson\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Refugio_County,_Texas" title="Refugio County, Texas">\n        Refugio\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/San_Patricio_County,_Texas" title="San Patricio County, Texas">\n        San Patricio\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Victoria_County,_Texas" title="Victoria County, Texas">\n        Victoria\n       </a>\n       counties, as well as parts of\n       <a href="/wiki/Matagorda_County,_Texas" title="Matagorda County, Texas">\n        Matagorda County\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Nestel_51-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Nestel-51">\n         [50]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On August\xc2\xa026, Governor Abbott added an additional 20\xc2\xa0counties to the state of emergency declaration.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Dart_52-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Dart-52">\n         [51]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Furthermore, the\n       <a href="/wiki/International_Charter_on_Space_and_Major_Disasters" title="International Charter on Space and Major Disasters">\n        International Charter on Space and Major Disasters\n       </a>\n       was activated by the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/USGS" title="USGS">\n        USGS\n       </a>\n       on behalf of the\n       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Governor%27s_Texas_Emergency_Management_Council&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Governor\'s Texas Emergency Management Council (page does not exist)">\n        Governor\'s Texas Emergency Management Council\n       </a>\n       , including the\n       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Texas_Division_of_Emergency_Management&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Texas Division of Emergency Management (page does not exist)">\n        Texas Division of Emergency Management\n       </a>\n       , thus providing for humanitarian satellite coverage.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Satellite_Coverage_Activated_for_Hurricane_Harvey_53-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Satellite_Coverage_Activated_for_Hurricane_Harvey-53">\n         [52]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Louisiana">\n        Louisiana\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Harvey&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Louisiana">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/Louisiana" title="Louisiana">\n        Louisiana\n       </a>\n       , Governor\n       <a href="/wiki/John_Bel_Edwards" title="John Bel Edwards">\n        John Bel Edwards\n       </a>\n       declared a state of emergency for the entire state. A mandatory evacuation was ordered in\n       <a href="/wiki/Cameron_Parish,_Louisiana" title="Cameron Parish, Louisiana">\n        Cameron Parish\n       </a>\n       for the cities of Big Lake,\n       <a href="/wiki/Cameron,_Louisiana" title="Cameron, Louisiana">\n        Cameron\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Creole,_Louisiana" title="Creole, Louisiana">\n        Creole\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Grand_Chenier,_Louisiana" title="Grand Chenier, Louisiana">\n        Grand Chenier\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Hackberry,_Louisiana" title="Hackberry, Louisiana">\n        Hackberry\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Holly_Beach,_Louisiana" title="Holly Beach, Louisiana">\n        Holly Beach\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Johnson_Bayou,_Louisiana" title="Johnson Bayou, Louisiana">\n        Johnson Bayou\n       </a>\n       . Additionally, a voluntary evacuation was ordered in\n       <a href="/wiki/Vermilion_Parish,_Louisiana" title="Vermilion Parish, Louisiana">\n        Vermilion Parish\n       </a>\n       for low-lying areas south of\n       <a href="/wiki/Louisiana_Highway_14" title="Louisiana Highway 14">\n        State Highway 14\n       </a>\n       . The\n       <a href="/wiki/Louisiana_National_Guard" title="Louisiana National Guard">\n        Louisiana National Guard\n       </a>\n       prepared about 500,000\xc2\xa0sandbags and emergency boats and high-water-rescue vehicles were placed on standby should flooding occur. In\n       <a href="/wiki/New_Orleans" title="New Orleans">\n        New Orleans\n       </a>\n       , there were concerns about whether or not the city\'s drainage system could handle a heavy rainfall event, with only 105\xc2\xa0of the 120\xc2\xa0water pumps being operational and some power turbines being out of service.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-54">\n        <a href="#cite_note-54">\n         [53]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The city\'s public schools, as well as six universities and a medical school, closed on August 29.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AP_SW_LA_55-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-AP_SW_LA-55">\n         [54]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As Harvey began re-emerging into the Gulf of Mexico on August\xc2\xa028, the tropical storm warning in Texas from Mesquite Bay to High Island was extended eastward into Louisiana to the community of Cameron at 12:00\xc2\xa0UTC, while a tropical storm watch was issued from Cameron to\n       <a href="/wiki/Intracoastal_City,_Louisiana" title="Intracoastal City, Louisiana">\n        Intracoastal City\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ad33_50-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ad33-50">\n         [49]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Effects_in_the_Caribbean_and_Latin_America">\n        Effects in the Caribbean and Latin America\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Harvey&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Effects in the Caribbean and Latin America">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       Winds left residents throughout\n       <a href="/wiki/Barbados" title="Barbados">\n        Barbados\n       </a>\n       without electricity, with a majority of outages occurring in\n       <a href="/wiki/Christ_Church,_Barbados" title="Christ Church, Barbados">\n        Christ Church\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Saint_Joseph,_Barbados" title="Saint Joseph, Barbados">\n        Saint Joseph\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Saint_Lucy,_Barbados" title="Saint Lucy, Barbados">\n        Saint Lucy\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Saint_Michael,_Barbados" title="Saint Michael, Barbados">\n        Saint Michael\n       </a>\n       provinces. Flooding washed one house off its foundation, while water entered some houses, forcing some people to evacuate. Bridges in\n       <a href="/wiki/Saint_Andrew,_Barbados" title="Saint Andrew, Barbados">\n        Saint Andrew\n       </a>\n       and Saint Joseph were damaged. Additionally, a fuel depot in\n       <a href="/wiki/Speightstown" title="Speightstown">\n        Speightstown\n       </a>\n       was flooded. Winds deroofed a church.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-56">\n        <a href="#cite_note-56">\n         [55]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/Saint_Vincent_and_the_Grenadines" title="Saint Vincent and the Grenadines">\n        Saint Vincent and the Grenadines\n       </a>\n       , nine homes were flooded and four others experienced wind damage. Also, a tree fell on a school, damaging the building. Blocked drains in\n       <a href="/wiki/Port_Elizabeth,_Saint_Vincent_and_the_Grenadines" title="Port Elizabeth, Saint Vincent and the Grenadines">\n        Port Elizabeth\n       </a>\n       resulted in more than 15\xc2\xa0businesses being flooded. A total of 15\xc2\xa0people were housed in shelters after the storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cdema_2-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-cdema-2">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Strong winds and heavy rainfall also affected\n       <a href="/wiki/Suriname" title="Suriname">\n        Suriname\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Guyana" title="Guyana">\n        Guyana\n       </a>\n       . In the former, high winds in the capital city of\n       <a href="/wiki/Paramaribo" title="Paramaribo">\n        Paramaribo\n       </a>\n       caused roof damage to the\n       <a href="/wiki/Presidential_Palace_of_Suriname" title="Presidential Palace of Suriname">\n        Presidential Palace\n       </a>\n       and two homes, while the Torarica Hotel and Casino suffered structural impact. Additionally, four dwellings were deroofed in\n       <a href="/wiki/Commewijne_District" title="Commewijne District">\n        Commewijne\n       </a>\n       and three others lost their roofs in\n       <a href="/wiki/Wanica_District" title="Wanica District">\n        Wanica\n       </a>\n       ; in the latter, the Ministry of Social Affairs building was damaged by falling trees. In Guyana, the village of Jawalla bore the brunt of the storm. Four homes were demolished, while five other residences and two shops were damaged. Several public buildings were also damaged, including the community center, the village council buildings, the nursery, and public schools. A 29-year-old woman died after her house collapsed on her.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cdema_2-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-cdema-2">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Effects_in_the_United_States">\n        Effects in the United States\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Harvey&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Effects in the United States">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Texas_2">\n        Texas\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Harvey&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Texas">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image"       <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Support_during_Hurricane_Harvey_(TX)_(50).jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Flooding in Texas on August 31\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Houston_Homeowners,_Small-business_Owners_Feel_Effects_of_Harvey.webm" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         \'Houston Homeowners, Small-business Owners Feel Effects of Harvey\' news report from\n         <a href="/wiki/Voice_of_America" title="Voice of America">\n          Voice of America\n         </a>\n         on September 4, 2017\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Throughout Texas, more than 300,000\xc2\xa0people were left without electricity and billions of dollars of property damage was sustained.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Dart_52-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Dart-52">\n         [51]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As of November 1, at least 89 fatalities have been confirmed, most of which were drownings.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Xinhua_Net_death_toll_4-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Xinhua_Net_death_toll-4">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Chron_death_toll_5-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Chron_death_toll-5">\n         [4]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Harvey_and_Irma_3-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Harvey_and_Irma-3">\n         [2]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-just_died_8-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-just_died-8">\n         [7]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       By August\xc2\xa029, 2017 approximately 13,000\xc2\xa0people had been rescued across the state while an estimated 30,000 were displaced.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WP_Aug29_57-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-WP_Aug29-57">\n         [56]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Economy_of_Houston#Petrochemicals" title="Economy of Houston">\n        refinery industry\n       </a>\n       capacity was reduced, and oil and gas production was affected in the Gulf of Mexico and inland Texas.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-58">\n        <a href="#cite_note-58">\n         [57]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On Monday, various news outlets announced the closure of oil refineries ahead of Hurricane Harvey, creating an artificial fuel shortage. Panicked, motorists waited in long lines. Consequently, gas stations through the state were forced to close due to the rush.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-59">\n        <a href="#cite_note-59">\n         [58]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       More than 20 percent of refining capacity was affected\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-60">\n        <a href="#cite_note-60">\n         [59]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       More than 48,700 homes were affected by Harvey throughout the state, including over 1,000 that were completely destroyed and more than 17,000 that sustained major damage; approximately 32,000 sustained minor damage. Nearly 700 businesses were damaged as well.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AP_61-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-AP-61">\n         [60]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Texas_Department_of_Public_Safety" title="Texas Department of Public Safety">\n        Texas Department of Public Safety\n       </a>\n       stated more than 185,000 homes were damaged and 9,000 destroyed.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-62">\n        <a href="#cite_note-62">\n         [61]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Landfall_area">\n        Landfall area\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <div class="PopUpMediaTransform" id="mwe_player_10"       <span class="play-btn-large">\n           <span class="mw-tmh-playtext">\n            Play media\n           </span>\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </div>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Coast_Guard_responds_after_Hurricane_Harvey_(546085).webm" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Coast Guard video during an overflight from\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Port_Aransas" title="Port Aransas">\n          Port Aransas\n         </a>\n         to\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Port_O%27Connor" title="Port O\'Connor">\n          Port O\'Connor\n         </a>\n         , Texas, Aug. 26, 2017\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Making landfall as a Category\xc2\xa04, Harvey inflicted tremendous damage across\n       <a href="/wiki/Aransas_County,_Texas" title="Aransas County, Texas">\n        Aransas County\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-TWC_Landfall_63-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-TWC_Landfall-63">\n         [62]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Wind gusts were observed up to 132\xc2\xa0mph (212\xc2\xa0km/h) near\n       <a href="/wiki/Port_Aransas,_Texas" title="Port Aransas, Texas">\n        Port Aransas\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WPC14_64-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-WPC14-64">\n         [63]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/Rockport,_Texas" title="Rockport, Texas">\n        Rockport\n       </a>\n       , entire blocks were leveled by the hurricane\'s winds. The city\'s courthouse was severely damaged when a\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cargo_trailer" title="Cargo trailer">\n        cargo trailer\n       </a>\n       was hurled into it, coming to a stop halfway through the structure. The gymnasium of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Rockport-Fulton_High_School" title="Rockport-Fulton High School">\n        Rockport-Fulton High School\n       </a>\n       lost multiple walls while the school itself suffered some damage.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-TWC_Landfall_63-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-TWC_Landfall-63">\n         [62]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A\n       <a href="/wiki/Fairfield_Inn_by_Marriott" title="Fairfield Inn by Marriott">\n        Fairfield Inn\n       </a>\n       in the city was severely damaged.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-65">\n        <a href="#cite_note-65">\n         [64]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       One person died in a house fire in the city, unable to be rescued due to the extreme weather conditions.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-66">\n        <a href="#cite_note-66">\n         [65]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As of August\xc2\xa028, an estimated 30\xe2\x80\x9340\xc2\xa0people remain unaccounted for across Aransas County, including 9 in Rockport. Nearly every structure in Port Aransas suffered damage.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-TWC_Landfall_63-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-TWC_Landfall-63">\n         [62]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       By the afternoon of August\xc2\xa026, more than 20\xc2\xa0in (51\xc2\xa0cm) of rain had fallen in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Corpus_Christi_metropolitan_area" title="Corpus Christi metropolitan area">\n        Corpus Christi metropolitan area\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Dart_52-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Dart-52">\n         [51]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       All of\n       <a href="/wiki/Victoria,_Texas" title="Victoria, Texas">\n        Victoria\n       </a>\n       was left without water and most had no power.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-TWC_Landfall_63-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-TWC_Landfall-63">\n         [62]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Houston_metropolitan_area_flooding">\n        Houston metropolitan area flooding\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Harvey&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Houston metropolitan area flooding">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <div style="float:left;clear:left;">\n       <div class="thumb tleft">\n        <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n         <div class="PopUpMediaTransform" id="mwe_player_12" style="width:220px;" videopayload="&lt;div class=&quot;mediaContainer&quot; data-height=&quot;360&quot; data-bandwidth=&quot;525312&quot; data-framerate=&quot;25&quot;/&gt;&lt;/video&gt;&lt;/div&gt;">\n          <img alt="File:We\'re continuing to tally rainfall accumulations in the storm\'s wake, as -Har....webm" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/We%27re_continuing_to_tally_rainfall_accumulations_in_the_storm%27s_wake%2C_as_-Har....webm/220px--We%27re_continuing_to_tally_rainfall_accumulations_in_the_storm%27s_wake%2C_as_-Har....webm.jpg" style="width:220px;height:124px"/>\n          <a href="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/f/fa/We%27re_continuing_to_tally_rainfall_accumulations_in_the_storm%27s_wake%2C_as_-Har....webm" target="new" title="Play media">\n           <span class="play-btn-large">\n            <span class="mw-tmh-playtext">\n             Play media\n            </span>\n           </span>\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <div class="thumbcaption">\n          <div class="magnify">\n           <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:We%27re_continuing_to_tally_rainfall_accumulations_in_the_storm%27s_wake,_as_-Har....webm" title="Enlarge">\n           </a>\n          </div>\n          Rainfall accumulation from August 23 through August 29. Animation by\n          <a href="/wiki/NASA" title="NASA">\n           NASA\n          </a>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Many locations in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Greater_Houston" title="Greater Houston">\n        Houston metropolitan area\n       </a>\n       observed at least 30\xc2\xa0in (76\xc2\xa0cm) of precipitation,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WPC_15_67-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-WPC_15-67">\n         [66]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       with a maximum of 64.58\xc2\xa0in (164.0\xc2\xa0cm) in\n       <a href="/wiki/Nederland,_Texas" title="Nederland, Texas">\n        Nederland\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Harvey_SHV_68-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Harvey_SHV-68">\n         [67]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       This makes Harvey the wettest tropical cyclone on record for both Texas and the United States,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-69">\n        <a href="#cite_note-69">\n         [68]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       surpassing the previous rainfall record held by\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Amelia_(1978)" title="Tropical Storm Amelia (1978)">\n        Tropical Storm Amelia\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-70">\n        <a href="#cite_note-70">\n         [69]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The local National Weather Service office in Houston observed all-time record daily rainfall accumulations on both August\xc2\xa026 and 27, measured at 14.4\xc2\xa0in (37\xc2\xa0cm) and 16.08\xc2\xa0in (40.8\xc2\xa0cm) respectively.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-71">\n        <a href="#cite_note-71">\n         [70]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Multiple flash flood emergencies were issued in the Houston area by the National Weather Service beginning the night of August 26. In Pearland, a suburb south of Houston, a report was made of 9.92" of rainfall in 90 minutes.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-72">\n        <a href="#cite_note-72">\n         [71]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The 39.11\xc2\xa0in (99.3\xc2\xa0cm) of rain in August made the month the wettest ever recorded in Houston since record keeping began in 1892, more than doubling the previous record of 19.21\xc2\xa0in (48.8\xc2\xa0cm) in June 2001.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-73">\n        <a href="#cite_note-73">\n         [72]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Storm_surge" title="Storm surge">\n        storm surge\n       </a>\n       peaked at 6 feet at\n       <a href="/wiki/Port_Lavaca,_Texas" title="Port Lavaca, Texas">\n        Port Lavaca\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-74">\n        <a href="#cite_note-74">\n         [73]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-75">\n        <a href="#cite_note-75">\n         [74]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       reducing outflow of rainwater from land to sea.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-76">\n        <a href="#cite_note-76">\n         [75]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       During the storm, more than 800\n       <a href="/wiki/Greater_Houston" title="Greater Houston">\n        Houston area\n       </a>\n       flights were canceled, including 704\xc2\xa0at\n       <a href="/wiki/George_Bush_Intercontinental_Airport" title="George Bush Intercontinental Airport">\n        George Bush Intercontinental Airport\n       </a>\n       and 123\xc2\xa0at\n       <a href="/wiki/William_P._Hobby_Airport" title="William P. Hobby Airport">\n        William P. Hobby Airport\n       </a>\n       . Both airports eventually closed.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-McLaughlin_77-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-McLaughlin-77">\n         [76]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Several tornadoes were spawned in the area, one of which damaged or destroyed the roofs of dozens of homes in\n       <a href="/wiki/Sienna_Plantation,_Texas" title="Sienna Plantation, Texas">\n        Sienna Plantation\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Dart_52-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Dart-52">\n         [51]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As of August\xc2\xa029, 14\xc2\xa0fatalities have been confirmed from flooding in the Houston area, including 6 from the same family who died when their van was swept off a flooded bridge.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-78">\n        <a href="#cite_note-78">\n         [77]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A police officer drowned while trying to escape rising waters.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-79">\n        <a href="#cite_note-79">\n         [78]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Texas_Army_National_Guard_Hurricane_Harvey_Response.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3102"
