</a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Texas_Army_National_Guard_Hurricane_Harvey_Response.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Soldiers with the Texas Army National Guard move through flooded Houston streets as floodwaters from Hurricane Harvey continue to rise.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Harvey_2017_rainfall.gif">\n         <img alt="" in the United States.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       An estimated 25\xe2\x80\x9330\xc2\xa0percent of Harris County\xe2\x80\x94roughly 444\xc2\xa0mi\n       <sup>\n        2\n       </sup>\n       (1,150\xc2\xa0km\n       <sup>\n        2\n       </sup>\n       ) of land\xe2\x80\x94was submerged.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WP_Aug29_57-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-WP_Aug29-57">\n         [56]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <div      <span class="play-btn-large">\n           <span class="mw-tmh-playtext">\n            Play media\n           </span>\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </div>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Harvey_Search_and_Rescue_Mission_(546955).webm" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         U.S. Navy Sailors conduct a search and rescue mission above a residence in Beaumont, Texas\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Late on August\xc2\xa027, a mandatory evacuation was issued for all of\n       <a href="/wiki/Bay_City,_Texas" title="Bay City, Texas">\n        Bay City\n       </a>\n       as model projections indicated the downtown area would be inundated by 10\xc2\xa0ft (3.0\xc2\xa0m) of water. Flooding was anticipated to cut off access to the city around 1:00\xc2\xa0p.m. CDT on August\xc2\xa028.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-80">\n        <a href="#cite_note-80">\n         [79]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Evacuations took place in\n       <a href="/wiki/Conroe,_Texas" title="Conroe, Texas">\n        Conroe\n       </a>\n       on August\xc2\xa028 following release of water from the Lake Conroe dam.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-81">\n        <a href="#cite_note-81">\n         [80]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On the morning on August\xc2\xa029, a levee along Columbia Lakes in Brazoria County was breached, prompting officials to urgently request for everyone in the area to evacuate.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-82">\n        <a href="#cite_note-82">\n         [81]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-83">\n        <a href="#cite_note-83">\n         [82]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       On August 28, the\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Army_Corps_of_Engineers" title="United States Army Corps of Engineers">\n        U.S. Army Corps of Engineers\n       </a>\n       began controlled water releases from\n       <a href="/wiki/Addicks_Reservoir" title="Addicks Reservoir">\n        Addicks\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Barker_Reservoir" title="Barker Reservoir">\n        Barker Reservoirs\n       </a>\n       in the Buffalo Bayou watershed in an attempt to manage flood levels in the immediate area. According to the local Corps commander, "It\xe2\x80\x99s going to be better to release the water through the gates directly into Buffalo Bayou as opposed to letting it go around the end and through additional neighborhoods and ultimately into the bayou." At the time the releases started, the reservoirs had been rising at more than 6 inches (15\xc2\xa0cm) per hour.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-84">\n        <a href="#cite_note-84">\n         [83]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Many people began evacuating the area, fearing a levee breach.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-85">\n        <a href="#cite_note-85">\n         [84]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Despite attempts to alleviate the water rise, the Addicks Reservoir reached capacity on the morning of August\xc2\xa029 and began spilling out.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-86">\n        <a href="#cite_note-86">\n         [85]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The NASA\n       <a href="/wiki/Johnson_Space_Center" title="Johnson Space Center">\n        Johnson Space Center\n       </a>\n       was closed to employees and visitors due to the flooding until September 5. Only the critical mission control staff remain and reside in the control rooms to monitor procedures of the\n       <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">\n        International Space Station\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-87">\n        <a href="#cite_note-87">\n         [86]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span id="Deep_East_Texas_and_Beaumont\xe2\x80\x93Port_Arthur_area">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Deep_East_Texas_and_Beaumont.E2.80.93Port_Arthur_area">\n        Deep East Texas and Beaumont\xe2\x80\x93Port Arthur area\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Harvey&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Deep East Texas and Beaumont\xe2\x80\x93Port Arthur area">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <table class="rquote floatright" role="presentation" style="border-collapse:collapse; border-style:none; float:right; margin:0.5em 0.75em; width:30%;">\n       <tr style="text-align:left; vertical-align:top;">\n        <td style="color:#b2b7f2; font-size:3.3em; font-family:\'Times New Roman\',serif; font-weight:bold; padding:4px 2px 2px; width:0.5em; line-height: 1em;">\n         \xe2\x80\x9c\n        </td>\n        <td style="padding:0 10px;">\n         Anyone who chooses to not [evacuate] cannot expect to be rescued and should write their social security numbers in permanent marker on their arm so their bodies can be identified. The loss of life and property is certain. GET OUT OR DIE!\n        </td>\n        <td style="color:#b2b7f2; font-size:3.3em; font-family:\'Times New Roman\',serif; font-weight:bold; padding:4px 2px 2px; text-align:right; vertical-align:bottom; width:0.5em; line-height: 1em;">\n         \xe2\x80\x9d\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td class="rquotecite" colspan="3" style="padding-top:10px; font-size:smaller; line-height:1em; text-align:right;">\n         <cite>\n          \xe2\x80\x94\xc2\xa0Jacques Blanchette, Tyler County Emergency Management\n          <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-88">\n           <a href="#cite_note-88">\n            [87]\n           </a>\n          </sup>\n         </cite>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Beaumont%E2%80%93Port_Arthur_metropolitan_area" title="Beaumont\xe2\x80\x93Port Arthur metropolitan area">\n        Beaumont\xe2\x80\x93Port Arthur metropolitan area\n       </a>\n       also experienced torrential precipitation, including 32.55\xc2\xa0in (82.7\xc2\xa0cm) of rainfall in\n       <a href="/wiki/Beaumont,_Texas" title="Beaumont, Texas">\n        Beaumont\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WPC_15_67-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-WPC_15-67">\n         [66]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Rising waters of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Neches_River" title="Neches River">\n        Neches River\n       </a>\n       caused the city to lose service from its main pump station, as well as its secondary water source in\n       <a href="/wiki/Hardin_County,_Texas" title="Hardin County, Texas">\n        Hardin County\n       </a>\n       , cutting water supply to the city for an unknown amount of time.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-89">\n        <a href="#cite_note-89">\n         [88]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Flooding to the north and east of the Houston area resulted in mandatory evacuations for portions of\n       <a href="/wiki/Liberty_County,_Texas" title="Liberty County, Texas">\n        Liberty\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Jefferson_County,_Texas" title="Jefferson County, Texas">\n        Jefferson\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Tyler_County,_Texas" title="Tyler County, Texas">\n        Tyler\n       </a>\n       counties, while\n       <a href="/wiki/Jasper_County,_Texas" title="Jasper County, Texas">\n        Jasper\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Newton_County,_Texas" title="Newton County, Texas">\n        Newton\n       </a>\n       counties were under a voluntary evacuation.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-90">\n        <a href="#cite_note-90">\n         [89]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       One death occurred in Beaumont when a woman exited her disabled vehicle, but was swept away.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-91">\n        <a href="#cite_note-91">\n         [90]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/Port_Arthur,_Texas" title="Port Arthur, Texas">\n        Port Arthur\n       </a>\n       , the mayor stated that the entire city was submerged by water. Hundreds of displaced residents went to the Robert A. "Bob" Bowers Civic Center for shelter, but they were evacuated again after the building began to flood. Water entered at least several hundreds of homes in Jefferson County.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-92">\n        <a href="#cite_note-92">\n         [91]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Louisiana_2">\n        Louisiana\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Harvey&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Louisiana">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Heavy rainfall extended eastward into Louisiana, with the state recording up to 14.88\xc2\xa0in (37.8\xc2\xa0cm) of precipitation near the town of\n       <a href="/wiki/Iowa,_Louisiana" title="Iowa, Louisiana">\n        Iowa\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WPC_15_67-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-WPC_15-67">\n         [66]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In the town of\n       <a href="/wiki/Lake_Charles,_Louisiana" title="Lake Charles, Louisiana">\n        Lake Charles\n       </a>\n       , water reached 4\xc2\xa0ft (1.2\xc2\xa0m) in height, with homes flooded and hundreds of people forced to evacuate in one neighborhood alone. Throughout the state, about 500\xc2\xa0people were rescued by August\xc2\xa028, while 269\xc2\xa0people went to a shelter in southwest Louisiana, about 200\xc2\xa0of whom were rescued from their homes.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-93">\n        <a href="#cite_note-93">\n         [92]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       An EF2 tornado near\n       <a href="/wiki/Evangeline,_Louisiana" title="Evangeline, Louisiana">\n        Evangeline\n       </a>\n       damaged four homes, one of which was destroyed. The tornado also damaged fences, a motorcycle, a pickup truck, and toppled three electrical poles.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-94">\n        <a href="#cite_note-94">\n         [93]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:ISS-52_Hurricane_Harvey_(7).jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2726" data-file-width="4096" height="200" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e5/ISS-52_Hurricane_Harvey_%287%29.jpg/300px-ISS-52_Hurricane_Harvey_%287%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e5/ISS-52_Hurricane_Harvey_%287%29.jpg/450px-ISS-52_Hurricane_Harvey_%287%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e5/ISS-52_Hurricane_Harvey_%287%29.jpg/600px-ISS-52_Hurricane_Harvey_%287%29.jpg 2x" width="300"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:ISS-52_Hurricane_Harvey_(7).jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Tropical Storm Harvey on August 28, as seen from the\n         <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">\n          ISS\n         </a>\n         , two days before making a third landfall in\n         <a href="/wiki/Cameron,_Louisiana" title="Cameron, Louisiana">\n          Cameron, Louisiana\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Elsewhere">\n        Elsewhere\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Harvey&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Elsewhere">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Harvey_2017-09-02_1825Z.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1868" data-file-width="2616" height="214" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ca/Harvey_2017-09-02_1825Z.jpg/300px-Harvey_2017-09-02_1825Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ca/Harvey_2017-09-02_1825Z.jpg/450px-Harvey_2017-09-02_1825Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ca/Harvey_2017-09-02_1825Z.jpg/600px-Harvey_2017-09-02_1825Z.jpg 2x" width="300"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Harvey_2017-09-02_1825Z.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Satellite image of Hurricane Harvey\'s remnants over the Eastern US, on September 2.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/Alabama" title="Alabama">\n        Alabama\n       </a>\n       , a tornado in the vicinity of\n       <a href="/wiki/Reform,_Alabama" title="Reform, Alabama">\n        Reform\n       </a>\n       damaged two homes and destroyed a barn along\n       <a href="/wiki/Alabama_State_Route_17" title="Alabama State Route 17">\n        State Route 17\n       </a>\n       , while four people were hospitalized for their injuries. A possible tornado in\n       <a href="/wiki/Lamar_County,_Alabama" title="Lamar County, Alabama">\n        Lamar County\n       </a>\n       near\n       <a href="/wiki/Kennedy,_Alabama" title="Kennedy, Alabama">\n        Kennedy\n       </a>\n       caused damage to trees and roofs.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-95">\n        <a href="#cite_note-95">\n         [94]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/Tennessee" title="Tennessee">\n        Tennessee\n       </a>\n       , more than 19,000\xc2\xa0people lost electricity in\n       <a href="/wiki/Memphis,_Tennessee" title="Memphis, Tennessee">\n        Memphis\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-96">\n        <a href="#cite_note-96">\n         [95]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Low-lying streets in the area were inundated with water. One indirect death occurred in Memphis due to a weather-related head-on collision of a car and a tractor trailer on\n       <a href="/wiki/Interstate_40" title="Interstate 40">\n        Interstate 40\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-The_Birmingham_News_6-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-The_Birmingham_News-6">\n         [5]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Heavy rainfall in\n       <a href="/wiki/Nashville,_Tennessee" title="Nashville, Tennessee">\n        Nashville\n       </a>\n       inundated a number of roads and flooded an apartment complex, resulting in the evacuation of 13\xc2\xa0people. Overall, about 50\xc2\xa0people in the city evacuated from flooded areas.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-97">\n        <a href="#cite_note-97">\n         [96]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Energy_production">\n        Energy production\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Harvey&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Energy production">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       See also:\n       <a href="/wiki/2017_Arkema_plant_explosion" title="2017 Arkema plant explosion">\n        2017 Arkema plant explosion\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Energy production in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Gulf_of_Mexico" title="Gulf of Mexico">\n        Gulf of Mexico\n       </a>\n       declined in the wake of Harvey by approximately 21% \xe2\x80\x94 378,633 barrels per day of the 1.75 million\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Barrel_of_oil" title="Barrel of oil">\n        barrels of oil\n       </a>\n       produced each day.\n       <a href="/wiki/Natural_gas" title="Natural gas">\n        Natural gas\n       </a>\n       production declined by about 25.71% \xe2\x80\x94 827.89 million metric standard cubic meters per day (MMSCFD). The\n       <a href="/wiki/Eagle_Ford_Group" title="Eagle Ford Group">\n        Eagle Ford Rock Formation\n       </a>\n       (shale oil and gas) in southern Texas reduced production by 300,000 to 500,000\n       <abbr title="barrels per day">\n        bpd\n       </abbr>\n       , according to the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Texas_Railroad_Commission" title="Texas Railroad Commission">\n        Texas Railroad Commission\n       </a>\n       . Many energy-related ports and terminals are closed, delaying about fourteen crude oil tankers. About 2.25 million bpd of refining capacity was offline for several days; that is about 12% of total US capacity, with refineries affected at Corpus Christi, and later\n       <a href="/wiki/Port_Arthur,_Texas" title="Port Arthur, Texas">\n        Port Arthur\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Beaumont,_Texas" title="Beaumont, Texas">\n        Beaumont\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Lake_Charles,_Louisiana" title="Lake Charles, Louisiana">\n        Lake Charles, Louisiana\n       </a>\n       . The price of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Brent_crude" title="Brent crude">\n        Brent crude\n       </a>\n       <i>\n        versus\n       </i>\n       <a href="/wiki/West_Texas_Intermediate" title="West Texas Intermediate">\n        West Texas Intermediate\n       </a>\n       crude oil achieved a split of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/USD" title="USD">\n        U.S.\xe2\x80\x89$\n       </a>\n       5.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2017-08-28_Stratfor_98-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-2017-08-28_Stratfor-98">\n         [97]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Two\n       <a href="/wiki/ExxonMobil" title="ExxonMobil">\n        ExxonMobil\n       </a>\n       refineries had to be shut down following related storm damage and releases of hazardous pollutants.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-99">\n        <a href="#cite_note-99">\n         [98]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Two oil storage tanks owned by\n       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Burlington_Resources_Oil_and_Gas&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Burlington Resources Oil and Gas (page does not exist)">\n        Burlington Resources Oil and Gas\n       </a>\n       collectively spilled 30,000\xc2\xa0gallons of crude in\n       <a href="/wiki/DeWitt_County,_Texas" title="DeWitt County, Texas">\n        DeWitt County\n       </a>\n       . An additional 8,500\xc2\xa0gallons of wastewater was spilled in the incidents.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-100">\n        <a href="#cite_note-100">\n         [99]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       On August 30, the CEO of\n       <a href="/wiki/Arkema" title="Arkema">\n        Arkema\n       </a>\n       warned one of its chemical plants in\n       <a href="/wiki/Crosby,_Texas" title="Crosby, Texas">\n        Crosby, Texas\n       </a>\n       , could explode or be subject to intense fire due to the loss of "critical refrigeration" of materials.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-101">\n        <a href="#cite_note-101">\n         [100]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       All workers at the facility and residents within 1.5\xc2\xa0mi (2.4\xc2\xa0km) were evacuated. Eight of the plant\'s nine refrigeration units failed without power, enabling the stored chemicals to decompose and become combustible. Two explosions occurred around 2:00\xc2\xa0a.m. on August\xc2\xa031; 21\xc2\xa0emergency personnel were briefly hospitalized.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-102">\n        <a href="#cite_note-102">\n         [101]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Due to the shutdown in refineries,\n       <a href="/wiki/Gasoline_and_diesel_usage_and_pricing" title="Gasoline and diesel usage and pricing">\n        gas prices\n       </a>\n       did see an increase nationwide.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-103">\n        <a href="#cite_note-103">\n         [102]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       However, the increase was not as\n       <a href="/wiki/Economic_effects_of_Hurricane_Katrina" title="Economic effects of Hurricane Katrina">\n        extensive as Hurricane Katrina\n       </a>\n       due to the development of more fuel-efficient vehicles as well as\n       <a href="/wiki/Hydraulic_fracturing" title="Hydraulic fracturing">\n        fracking\n       </a>\n       technology having been refined since Katrina to allow oil drilling in\n       <a href="/wiki/Shale_oil_extraction" title="Shale oil extraction">\n        shale\n       </a>\n       areas\n       <a href="/wiki/Marcellus_natural_gas_trend" title="Marcellus natural gas trend">\n        such as\n       </a>\n       the\n       <a href="/wiki/Marcellus_Formation" title="Marcellus Formation">\n        Marcellus Formation\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CBS_104-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CBS-104">\n         [103]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Additionally, Harvey\'s impact coincided with\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Labor_Day_Weekend" title="Labor Day Weekend">\n        Labor Day Weekend\n       </a>\n       , which sees a traditional increase in gas prices due to the heavy travel for that weekend.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-105">\n        <a href="#cite_note-105">\n         [104]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Nonetheless, the spike brought the highest gas prices in two years.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CBS_104-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CBS-104">\n         [103]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Sports">\n        Sports\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Harvey&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Sports">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Astros_Strong.png">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="305" data-file-width="305" height="120" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c6/Astros_Strong.png/120px-Astros_Strong.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c6/Astros_Strong.png/180px-Astros_Strong.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c6/Astros_Strong.png/240px-Astros_Strong.png 2x" width="120"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Astros_Strong.png" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         In the aftermath of the storm, the Houston Astros began wearing this patch during the 2017 season in support of the storm\'s victims in Houston. They eventually went on to win the\n         <a href="/wiki/2017_World_Series" title="2017 World Series">\n          World Series\n         </a>\n         .\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The flooding in Houston from the storm required the traditional\n       <a href="/wiki/Governor%27s_Cup_(Texas)" title="Governor\'s Cup (Texas)">\n        Governor\'s Cup\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Football_League" title="National Football League">\n        National Football League\n       </a>\n       preseason game between the\n       <a href="/wiki/Dallas_Cowboys" title="Dallas Cowboys">\n        Dallas Cowboys\n       </a>\n       and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Houston_Texans" title="Houston Texans">\n        Houston Texans\n       </a>\n       scheduled for August 31 to be moved from\n       <a href="/wiki/NRG_Stadium" title="NRG Stadium">\n        NRG Stadium\n       </a>\n       in Houston to\n       <a href="/wiki/AT%26T_Stadium" title="AT&amp;T Stadium">\n        AT&amp;T Stadium\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/Arlington,_Texas" title="Arlington, Texas">\n        Arlington, Texas\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-106">\n        <a href="#cite_note-106">\n         [105]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The game was later cancelled to allow the Houston Texans players to return to Houston after the storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-107">\n        <a href="#cite_note-107">\n         [106]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In addition, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Houston_Astros" title="Houston Astros">\n        Houston Astros\n       </a>\n       were forced to move their August 29\xe2\x80\x9331 series with the\n       <a href="/wiki/Texas_Rangers_(baseball)" title="Texas Rangers (baseball)">\n        Texas Rangers\n       </a>\n       from\n       <a href="/wiki/Minute_Maid_Park" title="Minute Maid Park">\n        Minute Maid Park\n       </a>\n       in Houston to\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropicana_Field" title="Tropicana Field">\n        Tropicana Field\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/St._Petersburg,_Florida" title="St. Petersburg, Florida">\n        St. Petersburg, Florida\n       </a>\n       ;\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-108">\n        <a href="#cite_note-108">\n         [107]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       ironically, just two weeks later,\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Irma" title="Hurricane Irma">\n        Hurricane Irma\n       </a>\n       would force the stadium\'s regular tenants, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Tampa_Bay_Rays" title="Tampa Bay Rays">\n        Tampa Bay Rays\n       </a>\n       , to move three home games to\n       <a href="/wiki/Citi_Field" title="Citi Field">\n        Citi Field\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/New_York_City" title="New York City">\n        New York City\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-109">\n        <a href="#cite_note-109">\n         [108]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In the aftermath, the\n       <a href="/wiki/2017_Houston_Astros_season" title="2017 Houston Astros season">\n        Houston Astros\n       </a>\n       began to wear patches which had the logo of the team with the word "Strong" on the bottom of the patch, as well as promoting the hashtag\n       <i>\n        Houston Strong\n       </i>\n       , prominently displaying them as the Astros won the\n       <a href="/wiki/2017_World_Series" title="2017 World Series">\n        2017 World Series\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-110">\n        <a href="#cite_note-110">\n         [109]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-111">\n        <a href="#cite_note-111">\n         [110]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Manager\n       <a href="/wiki/A._J._Hinch" title="A. J. Hinch">\n        A. J. Hinch\n       </a>\n       has stated in an interview that the team wasn\'t just playing for a title, but to help boost moral support for the city.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-112">\n        <a href="#cite_note-112">\n         [111]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The annual\n       <a href="/wiki/Texas_Kickoff" title="Texas Kickoff">\n        Texas Kickoff\n       </a>\n       game that was to feature\n       <a href="/wiki/2017_BYU_Cougars_football_team" title="2017 BYU Cougars football team">\n        BYU\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/2017_LSU_Tigers_football_team" title="2017 LSU Tigers football team">\n        LSU\n       </a>\n       to kick off the\n       <a href="/wiki/2017_NCAA_Division_I_FBS_football_season" title="2017 NCAA Division I FBS football season">\n        2017 college football season\n       </a>\n       was moved to the\n       <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_Superdome" title="Mercedes-Benz Superdome">\n        Mercedes-Benz Superdome\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/New_Orleans" title="New Orleans">\n        New Orleans, Louisiana\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-113">\n        <a href="#cite_note-113">\n         [112]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The NCAA FBS football game between\n       <a href="/wiki/2017_Houston_Cougars_football_team" title="2017 Houston Cougars football team">\n        Houston\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/2017_UTSA_Roadrunners_football_team" title="2017 UTSA Roadrunners football team">\n        UTSA\n       </a>\n       was postponed due to the aftermath of the storm. It was originally scheduled for September 2 at the\n       <a href="/wiki/Alamodome" title="Alamodome">\n        Alamodome\n       </a>\n       in San Antonio and is expected to be rescheduled.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-114">\n        <a href="#cite_note-114">\n         [113]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Houston_Dynamo" title="Houston Dynamo">\n        Houston Dynamo\n       </a>\n       rescheduled a planned\n       <a href="/wiki/Major_League_Soccer" title="Major League Soccer">\n        Major League Soccer\n       </a>\n       match against\n       <a href="/wiki/Sporting_Kansas_City" title="Sporting Kansas City">\n        Sporting Kansas City\n       </a>\n       on August 26 to October 11. The\n       <a href="/wiki/Houston_Dash" title="Houston Dash">\n        Houston Dash\n       </a>\n       of the\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Women%27s_Soccer_League" title="National Women\'s Soccer League">\n        National Women\'s Soccer League\n       </a>\n       rescheduled their August 27 match against the\n       <a href="/wiki/North_Carolina_Courage" title="North Carolina Courage">\n        North Carolina Courage\n       </a>\n       to a date that has not been announced.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-115">\n        <a href="#cite_note-115">\n         [114]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Both teams moved their training camps to\n       <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Stadium_(Texas)" title="Toyota Stadium (Texas)">\n        Toyota Stadium\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/Frisco,_Texas" title="Frisco, Texas">\n        Frisco, Texas\n       </a>\n       (near Dallas) while preparing for their next matches; the Dash\'s match the following week, against the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Seattle_Reign" title="Seattle Reign">\n        Seattle Reign\n       </a>\n       , will be played in Frisco, with all proceeds from ticket sales benefiting an\n       <a href="/wiki/American_Red_Cross" title="American Red Cross">\n        American Red Cross\n       </a>\n       relief fund for hurricane victims.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-116">\n        <a href="#cite_note-116">\n         [115]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The Dynamo and Major League Soccer also donated a combined $1 million into the hurricane relief fund, while also opening\n       <a href="/wiki/BBVA_Compass_Stadium" title="BBVA Compass Stadium">\n        BBVA Compass Stadium\n       </a>\n       to accept donated supplies for processing and distribution.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-117">\n        <a href="#cite_note-117">\n         [116]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-118">\n        <a href="#cite_note-118">\n         [117]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Athletic events were rescheduled as far away as\n       <a href="/wiki/Kentucky" title="Kentucky">\n        Kentucky\n       </a>\n       , where the storm\'s remnants were expected to cause heavy rains on September 1, interfering with Friday night\n       <a href="/wiki/High_school_football" title="High school football">\n        high school football\n       </a>\n       . More than 50 high schools in the state moved games that had been scheduled for Friday to either Thursday or Saturday.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-119">\n        <a href="#cite_note-119">\n         [118]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Aftermath">\n        Aftermath\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Harvey&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Aftermath">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n
