id="Texas_3">\n        Texas\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Harvey&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Texas">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <div class="mediaContainer" style="width:220px">\n         <audio class="kskin" controls="" data-durationhint="429.94068027211" data-mwprovider="wikimediacommons" data-mwtitle="Houston_Mayor_Sylvester_Turner_Says_Houston_Begins_Recovery_Mission_-_Morning_Joe_-_MSNBC.ogg" data-startoffset="0" id="mwe_player_18" preload="none" style="width:220px">\n          <source data-bandwidth="127647" data-height="0" data-shorttitle="Ogg source" data-title="Original Ogg file (128 kbps)" data-width="0" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/d/d5/Houston_Mayor_Sylvester_Turner_Says_Houston_Begins_Recovery_Mission_-_Morning_Joe_-_MSNBC.ogg" type=\'audio/ogg; codecs="vorbis"\'/>\n          <track data-dir="ltr" data-mwprovider="wikimediacommons" data-mwtitle="TimedText:Houston_Mayor_Sylvester_Turner_Says_Houston_Begins_Recovery_Mission_-_Morning_Joe_-_MSNBC.ogg.en.srt" kind="subtitles" label="English (en) subtitles" src="https://commons.wikimedia.org/w/index.php?title=TimedText:Houston_Mayor_Sylvester_Turner_Says_Houston_Begins_Recovery_Mission_-_Morning_Joe_-_MSNBC.ogg.en.srt&amp;action=raw&amp;ctype=text%2Fx-srt" srclang="en" type="text/x-srt"/>\n         </audio>\n        </div>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Houston_Mayor_Sylvester_Turner_Says_Houston_Begins_Recovery_Mission_-_Morning_Joe_-_MSNBC.ogg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Interview with\n         <a href="/wiki/Sylvester_Turner" title="Sylvester Turner">\n          Sylvester Turner\n         </a>\n         and\n         <a href="/wiki/Al_Sharpton" title="Al Sharpton">\n          Al Sharpton\n         </a>\n         on September 1st 2017 \xe2\x80\x93 from\n         <a href="/wiki/MSNBC" title="MSNBC">\n          MSNBC\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Houston Mayor\n       <a href="/wiki/Sylvester_Turner" title="Sylvester Turner">\n        Sylvester Turner\n       </a>\n       imposed a mandatory\n       <a href="/wiki/Curfew" title="Curfew">\n        curfew\n       </a>\n       on August\xc2\xa029 from 12\xc2\xa0a.m. to 5\xc2\xa0a.m.\n       <a href="/wiki/Central_Time_Zone" title="Central Time Zone">\n        local time\n       </a>\n       until further notice. He cited looting as the primary reason for the curfew.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-124">\n        <a href="#cite_note-124">\n         [122]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On August\xc2\xa029, President Trump,\n       <a href="/wiki/First_Lady_of_the_United_States" title="First Lady of the United States">\n        First Lady\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Melania_Trump" title="Melania Trump">\n        Melania Trump\n       </a>\n       , and U.S. Senators\n       <a href="/wiki/John_Cornyn" title="John Cornyn">\n        John Cornyn\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Ted_Cruz" title="Ted Cruz">\n        Ted Cruz\n       </a>\n       toured damage in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Corpus_Christi_metropolitan_area" title="Corpus Christi metropolitan area">\n        Corpus Christi metropolitan area\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-125">\n        <a href="#cite_note-125">\n         [123]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       President Trump made a formal request for $5.95\xc2\xa0billion in federal funding on August\xc2\xa031 for affected areas, the vast majority of which would go to FEMA.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-126">\n        <a href="#cite_note-126">\n         [124]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Texas\n       <a href="/wiki/Governor_(United_States)" title="Governor (United States)">\n        Governor\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Greg_Abbott" title="Greg Abbott">\n        Greg Abbott\n       </a>\n       deployed the state\'s entire National Guard for search and rescue, recovery, and clean up operations due to the devastating damage caused by the storm and resulting floods.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-127">\n        <a href="#cite_note-127">\n         [125]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-128">\n        <a href="#cite_note-128">\n         [126]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Other states\' National Guard\'s have offered assistance, with several having already been sent.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-129">\n        <a href="#cite_note-129">\n         [127]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-130">\n        <a href="#cite_note-130">\n         [128]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Meanwhile, the United States Immigration and Customs Enforcement assigned approximately 150 employees from around the country to assist with disaster relief efforts, while stating that no immigration enforcement operations would be conducted.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AP_61-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-AP-61">\n         [60]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Approximately 32,000\xc2\xa0people were displaced in shelters across the state by August\xc2\xa031. The\n       <a href="/wiki/George_R._Brown_Convention_Center" title="George R. Brown Convention Center">\n        George R. Brown Convention Center\n       </a>\n       , the state\'s largest shelter, reached capacity with 8,000\xc2\xa0evacuees. The\n       <a href="/wiki/NRG_Center" title="NRG Center">\n        NRG Center\n       </a>\n       opened as a large public shelter accordingly. More than 210,000\xc2\xa0people registered with\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/FEMA" title="FEMA">\n        FEMA\n       </a>\n       for disaster assistance.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NYT_Aug30Live_131-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NYT_Aug30Live-131">\n         [129]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Cajun_Navy" title="Cajun Navy">\n        Cajun Navy\n       </a>\n       , an informal organization of volunteers with boats from Louisiana, deployed to Texas to assist in high-water rescues.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-132">\n        <a href="#cite_note-132">\n         [130]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The Houston Independent School District announced that all students on any of the district\'s campuses would be eligible for free lunch throughout the 2017\xe2\x80\x9318 school year. The Federal Department of Education eased financial aid rules and procedures for those affected by Harvey, giving schools the ability to waive paperwork requirements; loan borrowers were given more flexibility in managing their loan payments.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AP_61-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-AP-61">\n         [60]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A 36-year-old inmate sentenced to death for a 2003 murder was granted a temporary reprieve as a result of Harvey, as his legal team was based in Harris County, an area heavily affected by the hurricane.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AP_61-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-AP-61">\n         [60]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       By August\xc2\xa030, corporations across the nation collectively donated more than $72\xc2\xa0million to relief efforts, with 42\xc2\xa0companies donating at least $1\xc2\xa0million.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-133">\n        <a href="#cite_note-133">\n         [131]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Professional athletic teams, their players, and managers provided large donations to assist victims of the storm. The\n       <a href="/wiki/Houston_Astros" title="Houston Astros">\n        Houston Astros\n       </a>\n       pledged $4\xc2\xa0million to relief along with all proceeds from their home game raffles.\n       <a href="/wiki/Houston_Rockets" title="Houston Rockets">\n        Houston Rockets\n       </a>\n       owner\n       <a href="/wiki/Leslie_Alexander_(businessman)" title="Leslie Alexander (businessman)">\n        Leslie Alexander\n       </a>\n       also donated $4\xc2\xa0million to the cause.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-134">\n        <a href="#cite_note-134">\n         [132]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A fundraiser established by\n       <a href="/wiki/Houston_Texans" title="Houston Texans">\n        Houston Texans\n       </a>\n       defensive lineman\n       <a href="/wiki/J._J._Watt" title="J. J. Watt">\n        J. J. Watt\n       </a>\n       exceeded $37\xc2\xa0million.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-135">\n        <a href="#cite_note-135">\n         [133]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Texas_Rangers_(baseball)" title="Texas Rangers (baseball)">\n        Texas Rangers\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Tennessee_Titans" title="Tennessee Titans">\n        Tennessee Titans\n       </a>\n       both provided $1\xc2\xa0million, while the\n       <a href="/wiki/New_England_Patriots" title="New England Patriots">\n        New England Patriots\n       </a>\n       pledged to match up to $1\xc2\xa0million in donations to the Red Cross.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-136">\n        <a href="#cite_note-136">\n         [134]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Multiple Hollywood celebrities also pitched in, collectively donating more than $10\xc2\xa0million, with\n       <a href="/wiki/Sandra_Bullock" title="Sandra Bullock">\n        Sandra Bullock\n       </a>\n       providing the largest single donation of $1\xc2\xa0million.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-137">\n        <a href="#cite_note-137">\n         [135]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Leonardo_DiCaprio" title="Leonardo DiCaprio">\n        Leonardo DiCaprio\n       </a>\n       provided $1\xc2\xa0million to the United Way Harvey Recovery Fund through\n       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Leonardo_DiCaprio_Foundation&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Leonardo DiCaprio Foundation (page does not exist)">\n        his foundation\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-138">\n        <a href="#cite_note-138">\n         [136]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       President\n       <a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump" title="Donald Trump">\n        Donald Trump\n       </a>\n       reportedly donated $1\xc2\xa0million to 12 charities involved in relief efforts.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-139">\n        <a href="#cite_note-139">\n         [137]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Rachael_Ray" title="Rachael Ray">\n        Rachael Ray\n       </a>\n       provided donations totaling $1\xc2\xa0million to animal shelters across the Houston area.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-140">\n        <a href="#cite_note-140">\n         [138]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Economic_loss_estimates">\n        Economic loss estimates\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Harvey&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Economic loss estimates">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:President_Trump_signing_Hurricane_Harvey_bill_(cropped).jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1127" data-file-width="1256" height="197" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/President_Trump_signing_Hurricane_Harvey_bill_%28cropped%29.jpg/220px-President_Trump_signing_Hurricane_Harvey_bill_%28cropped%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/President_Trump_signing_Hurricane_Harvey_bill_%28cropped%29.jpg/330px-President_Trump_signing_Hurricane_Harvey_bill_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/President_Trump_signing_Hurricane_Harvey_bill_%28cropped%29.jpg/440px-President_Trump_signing_Hurricane_Harvey_bill_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:President_Trump_signing_Hurricane_Harvey_bill_(cropped).jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         President Trump signs H.R. 601 into effect providing $15 billion in disaster relief for hurricane victims\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/Moody%27s_Analytics" title="Moody\'s Analytics">\n        Moody\'s Analytics\n       </a>\n       initially estimated the total economic cost of the storm at $81 billion to $108 billion or more; most of the economic losses are damage to homes and commercial property.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Lee_141-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Lee-141">\n         [139]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/USA_Today" title="USA Today">\n         USA Today\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       reported an\n       <a href="/wiki/AccuWeather" title="AccuWeather">\n        AccuWeather\n       </a>\n       estimate of $190 billion, released August 31.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-190billion_142-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-190billion-142">\n         [140]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On September 3, Texas state governor Greg Abbott estimated that damages will be between $150\xc2\xa0billion and $180\xc2\xa0billion, surpassing the $120\xc2\xa0billion that it took to rebuild\n       <a href="/wiki/New_Orleans" title="New Orleans">\n        New Orleans\n       </a>\n       after Katrina.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-180_billion_143-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-180_billion-143">\n         [141]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-144">\n        <a href="#cite_note-144">\n         [142]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       According to weather analytics firm\n       <a href="/wiki/Planalytics" title="Planalytics">\n        Planalytics\n       </a>\n       , lost revenue to Houston area retailers and restaurants alone will be approximately $1 billion. The Houston area controls 4% of the spending power in the United States.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-145">\n        <a href="#cite_note-145">\n         [143]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In September 2017, the Insurance Council of Texas estimated the total insured losses from Hurricane Harvey at $19 billion. This figure represents $11 billion in flood losses insured by the\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Flood_Insurance_Program" title="National Flood Insurance Program">\n        National Flood Insurance Program\n       </a>\n       (NFIP), $3 billion in "insured windstorm and other storm-related property losses"; and about $4.75 billion in insured flood losses of private and commercial vehicles.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-146">\n        <a href="#cite_note-146">\n         [144]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In early November 2017, Ball State University compiled a preliminary damage report for Hurricane Harvey, with the total costs reaching at least $198.63 billion (2017 USD). This makes Hurricane Harvey the costliest tropical cyclone on record, surpassing\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Katrina" title="Hurricane Katrina">\n        Hurricane Katrina\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-198billion_9-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-198billion-9">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       A significant portion of the storm\'s damages are uninsured losses. Regular homeowner insurance policies generally exclude coverage for flooding, as the NFIP underwrites most flood insurance policies in the US.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NYT:_NFIP_147-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NYT:_NFIP-147">\n         [145]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CNN:_Lack_of_flood_insurance_148-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CNN:_Lack_of_flood_insurance-148">\n         [146]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Although the purchase of flood insurance is obligatory for federally guaranteed mortgages for homes within the\n       <a href="/wiki/100-year_flood" title="100-year flood">\n        100-year flood plain\n       </a>\n       , enforcement of the requirement is difficult and many homes, even within the 100-year flood plain, lack flood insurance.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NYT:_NFIP_147-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NYT:_NFIP-147">\n         [145]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/Harris_County,_Texas" title="Harris County, Texas">\n        Harris County, Texas\n       </a>\n       \xe2\x80\x94which includes the city of Houston\xe2\x80\x94only 15% of homes have flood insurance policies issued by the NFIP. Participation in the NFIP is higher, but still low, in neighboring\n       <a href="/wiki/Galveston_County,_Texas" title="Galveston County, Texas">\n        Galveston\n       </a>\n       (41%),\n       <a href="/wiki/Brazoria_County,_Texas" title="Brazoria County, Texas">\n        Brazoria\n       </a>\n       (26%), and\n       <a href="/wiki/Chambers_County,_Texas" title="Chambers County, Texas">\n        Chambers Counties\n       </a>\n       (21%).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NYT:_NFIP_147-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NYT:_NFIP-147">\n         [145]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Homeowners sued authorities after reservoir releases damaged homes.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-149">\n        <a href="#cite_note-149">\n         [147]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Federal_government_response">\n        Federal government response\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Harvey&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Federal government response">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       On September 8, President\n       <a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump" title="Donald Trump">\n        Donald Trump\n       </a>\n       signed into law H.R. 601, which among other spending actions designated $15 billion for Hurricane Harvey relief.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-150">\n        <a href="#cite_note-150">\n         [148]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Non-governmental_organization_response">\n        Non-governmental organization response\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Harvey&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Non-governmental organization response">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/American_Red_Cross" title="American Red Cross">\n        American Red Cross\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Salvation_Army" title="Salvation Army">\n        Salvation Army\n       </a>\n       , United Methodist Committee on Relief (UMCOR)\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Equestrian_Federation" title="United States Equestrian Federation">\n        United States Equestrian Federation\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Humane_Society_of_the_United_States" title="Humane Society of the United States">\n        Humane Society of the United States\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Knights_of_Columbus" title="Knights of Columbus">\n        Knights of Columbus\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Catholic_Charities_USA" title="Catholic Charities USA">\n        Catholic Charities USA\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/AmeriCares" title="AmeriCares">\n        AmeriCares\n       </a>\n       , Operation BBQ relief, many celebrities, and many other charitable organizations provided help to the victims of the storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SalvArmy_151-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SalvArmy-151">\n         [149]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Equine_152-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Equine-152">\n         [150]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-PetsRescue_153-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-PetsRescue-153">\n         [151]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Anarchism" title="Anarchism">\n        Anarchists\n       </a>\n       (including\n       <a href="/wiki/Antifa_(United_States)" title="Antifa (United States)">\n        Antifa\n       </a>\n       ) also provided relief.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Anarchists_.26_Antifa_Relief_154-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Anarchists_.26_Antifa_Relief-154">\n         [152]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Business aviation played a part in the rescue efforts, providing support during the storm as well as relief flights bringing in suppliers in the immediate aftermath.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-155">\n        <a href="#cite_note-155">\n         [153]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Volunteers from\n       <a href="/wiki/Amateur_radio" title="Amateur radio">\n        amateur radio\n       </a>\n       \'s emergency service wing, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Amateur_Radio_Emergency_Service" title="Amateur Radio Emergency Service">\n        Amateur Radio Emergency Service\n       </a>\n       , provided communications in\n       <a href="/wiki/American_Red_Cross" title="American Red Cross">\n        American Red Cross\n       </a>\n       shelters in South Texas.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ARRLSupt_156-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ARRLSupt-156">\n         [154]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Many corporations also contributed to relief efforts. Operation BBQ relief had the help from several local individuals and businesses kick off the support of providing meals for volunteers and victims. Smokers, pallets of wood, and another company came up with the pounds of pork to kick off the support effort.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SmokdMeat_157-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SmokdMeat-157">\n         [155]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Although Operation BBQ relief has been in effect since May 2011 with the\n       <a href="/wiki/2011_Joplin_tornado" title="2011 Joplin tornado">\n        2011 Joplin tornado\n       </a>\n       , they estimate the Houston 2017 relief project to be their biggest ever.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Operation BBQ relief vendors volunteering for the Houston flood relief estimates that they will serve at least 450,000 meals.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BBQRelief_158-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-BBQRelief-158">\n         [156]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On August 27, 2017 it was estimated that Operation BBQ relief will be expecting 25,000 to 30,000 meals a day.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Ready2Help_159-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Ready2Help-159">\n         [157]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       On August 27, 2017\n       <a href="/wiki/KSL-TV" title="KSL-TV">\n        KSL-TV\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/KSL_(radio)" title="KSL (radio)">\n        KSL Newsradio\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/KSFI" title="KSFI">\n        FM100.3\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/KRSP-FM" title="KRSP-FM">\n        103.5 The Arrow\n       </a>\n       created a fundraiser to help Texas residents impacted by Hurricane Harvey. Because of an anonymous donor willing to match $2 for every $1 raised up to a total of $100,000,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Peter_Huntsman" title="Peter Huntsman">\n        Peter Huntsman\n       </a>\n       also agreed to match donations up to $100,000. The combined total of $200,000 was met by August 31, 2017. Their new goal is $1 million.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-KSLFundzr_160-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-KSLFundzr-160">\n         [158]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Foreign_government_response">\n        Foreign government response\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Harvey&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Foreign government response">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/Singapore" title="Singapore">\n        Singapore\n       </a>\n       dispatched\n       <a href="/wiki/Boeing_CH-47_Chinook" title="Boeing CH-47 Chinook">\n        Boeing CH-47 Chinook\n       </a>\n       helicopters from the\n       <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Singapore_Air_Force" title="Republic of Singapore Air Force">\n        Republic of Singapore Air Force\n       </a>\n       to areas affected by the hurricane for humanitarian operations, working alongside the Texas National Guard.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CNA_161-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CNA-161">\n         [159]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">\n        Israel\n       </a>\n       pledged $1 million in relief funds for restoration of non-state run communal infrastructure.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-162">\n        <a href="#cite_note-162">\n         [160]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">\n        Mexico\n       </a>\n       sent volunteers from the\n       <a href="/wiki/Mexican_Red_Cross" title="Mexican Red Cross">\n        Mexican Red Cross\n       </a>\n       , firemen from\n       <a href="/wiki/Coahuila" title="Coahuila">\n        Coahuila\n       </a>\n       , and rescue teams from\n       <a href="/wiki/Guanajuato" title="Guanajuato">\n        Guanajuato\n       </a>\n       to Houston to assist in relief.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-163">\n        <a href="#cite_note-163">\n         [161]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Mexico later rescinded their commitment for aid after Hurricane Katia made landfall on Mexico\'s Gulf Coast, on September 9, 2017.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-rescinds_aid_164-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-rescinds_aid-164">\n         [162]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">\n        Venezuela\n       </a>\n       offered $5 million through the state-owned\n       <a href="/wiki/Citgo" title="Citgo">\n        Citgo Petroleum\n       </a>\n       , which operates a refinery in Corpus Christi.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-165">\n        <a href="#cite_note-165">\n         [163]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Health_and_environmental_hazards_in_flood_waters">\n        Health and environmental hazards in flood waters\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Harvey&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Health and environmental hazards in flood waters">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The floodwaters contain a number of hazards to the environment and human health. The Houston Health Department stated that "millions of contaminants" were present in floodwaters.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-TabuchiKaplan_166-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-TabuchiKaplan-166">\n         [164]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       These include\n       <i>\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/E._coli" title="E. coli">\n         E. coli\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Coliform" title="Coliform">\n        coliform\n       </a>\n       bacteria; measurements of\n       <a href="/wiki/Colony-forming_unit" title="Colony-forming unit">\n        colony-forming units\n       </a>\n       showed the concentrations were so high that there were risks of contracting\n       <a href="/wiki/Necrotizing_fasciitis" title="Necrotizing fasciitis">\n        flesh-eating disease\n       </a>\n       from the water.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-167">\n        <a href="#cite_note-167">\n         [165]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Houston officials stated that the Houston drinking water and sewer systems were intact; however, "hundreds of thousands of people across the 38 Texas counties affected by Hurricane Harvey use private wells, according to an estimate by\n       <a href="/wiki/Louisiana_State_University" title="Louisiana State University">\n        Louisiana State University\n       </a>\n       researchers, and those people must fend for themselves."\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-TabuchiKaplan_166-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-TabuchiKaplan-166">\n         [164]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Additionally,\n       <a href="/wiki/Harris_County,_Texas" title="Harris County, Texas">\n        Harris County\n       </a>\n       , which includes Houston, contains a large number of\n       <a href="/wiki/Superfund" title="Superfund">\n        Superfund\n       </a>\n       -designed\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Brownfield" title="Brownfield">\n        brownfield\n       </a>\n       sites that contain a wide variety of toxins and carcinogens.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-TabuchiKaplan_166-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-TabuchiKaplan-166">\n         [164]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Two Superfund sites in Corpus Christi were flooded.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-TabuchiKaplan_166-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-TabuchiKaplan-166">\n         [164]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Environmental_factors">\n        Environmental factors\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Harvey&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Environmental factors">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Geography_of_Houston" title="Geography of Houston">\n        Geography of Houston\n       </a>\n       places it in a low-lying part of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Gulf_Coastal_Plain" title="Gulf Coastal Plain">\n        Gulf Coastal Plain\n       </a>\n       , and its\n       <a href="/wiki/Clay" title="Clay">\n        clay\n       </a>\n       -based soils provide poor drainage. The\n       <a href="/wiki/Climate_of_Houston" title="Climate of Houston">\n        climate of Houston\n       </a>\n       brings very heavy rainfall, which together with tidal flood events means that there have been repeated floods in the city ever since its founding in 1836, though the flood control district founded in 1947, aided by the\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Army_Corps_of_Engineers" title="United States Army Corps of Engineers">\n        U.S. Army Corps of Engineers\n       </a>\n       , managed to prevent statewide flooding for over fifty years. More recently, residents died in "historic flooding" in\n       <a href="/wiki/2015_Texas%E2%80%93Oklahoma_flood_and_tornado_outbreak" title="2015 Texas\xe2\x80\x93Oklahoma flood and tornado outbreak">\n        May 2015\n       </a>\n       , and in the\n       <a href="/wiki/April_2016_North_American_storm_complex" title="April 2016 North American storm complex">\n        April 2016 "tax day floods"\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Gabbatt_2808_168-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Gabbatt_2808-168">\n         [166]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Fox_29082017_169-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Fox_29082017-169">\n         [167]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       There is a tendency for storms to move very slowly over the region, and drop huge amounts of rain over an extended period, as occurred during\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Claudette_(1979)" title="Tropical Storm Claudette (1979)">\n        Tropical Storm Claudette\n       </a>\n       in 1979, and\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Allison" title="Tropical Storm Allison">\n        Tropical Storm Allison\n       </a>\n       in 2001.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NPR.org_28_8_2017_170-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NPR.org_28_8_2017-170">\n         [168]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The area is a very flat flood plain at shallow gradient, slowly draining rainwater through an intricate network of channels and bayous to the sea. The main waterways, the\n       <a href="/wiki/San_Jacinto_River_(Texas)" title="San Jacinto River (Texas)">\n        San Jacinto River\n       </a>\n       and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Buffalo_Bayou" title="Buffalo Bayou">\n        Buffalo Bayou\n       </a>\n       , meander slowly, laden with mud, and have little capacity for carrying storm water.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Vartabedian_2017_171-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Vartabedian_2017-171">\n         [169]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Urban_development">\n        Urban development\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Harvey&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Urban development">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Houston has seen rapid urban development (\n       <a href="/wiki/Urban_sprawl" title="Urban sprawl">\n        urban sprawl\n       </a>\n       ), with absorbent prairie and wetlands replaced by hard surfaces which rapidly shed storm water, overwhelming the drainage capacity of the rivers and channels.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Fernandez_Fausset_2017_172-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Fernandez_Fausset_2017-172">\n         [170]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Between 1992 and 2010, almost 25,000 acres of wetlands were lost, decreasing the detention capacity of the region by four billion gallons.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-173">\n        <a href="#cite_note-173">\n         [171]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       However, Harvey was estimated to have dropped more than fifteen trillion gallons of water in the area.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-174">\n        <a href="#cite_note-174">\n         [172]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The Katy Prairie in western Harris County, which once helped to absorb floodwaters in the region, has been reduced to one quarter of its previous size in the last several decades due to\n       <a href="/wiki/Urban_sprawl" title="Urban sprawl">\n        suburban development\n       </a>\n       , and one analysis discovered that more than 7,000 housing units have been built within the 100-year floodplain in Harris County since 2010.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-175">\n        <a href="#cite_note-175">\n         [173]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Subsidence">\n        Subsidence\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Harvey&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Subsidence">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Extraction of oil and groundwater from underground\n       <a href="/wiki/Aquifer" title="Aquifer">\n        aquifers\n       </a>\n       leaves unsupported voids resulting in ground collapse, a process called\n       <a href="/wiki/Subsidence" title="Subsidence">\n        subsidence\n       </a>\n       . Houston itself is in a very large subsidence bowl, with smaller bowls within that area showing greater subsidence: in some cases as much as 9 feet (2.7\xc2\xa0m). These result in drainage systems no longer having the required gradient to operate efficiently, so storm water drains more slowly.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Harden_losing_ground_176-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Harden_losing_ground-176">\n         [174]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The coastline near Houston has seen sea level increasing by 6 inches (15\xc2\xa0cm) in recent decades due to subsidence combined with the\n       <a href="/wiki/Sea_level_rise" title="Sea level rise">\n        effects of climate change\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Mann2817_177-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Mann2817-177">\n         [175]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Harden_losing_ground_176-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Harden_losing_ground-176">\n         [174]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Climate_change">\n        Climate change\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Harvey&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Climate change">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       See also:\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone#Climate_change" title="Tropical cyclone">\n        Tropical cyclone \xc2\xa7\xc2\xa0Climate change\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Gulf_of_Mexico" title="Gulf of Mexico">\n        Gulf of Mexico\n       </a>\n       is known for hurricanes in August, so their incidence alone cannot be attributed to\n       <a href="/wiki/Global_warming" title="Global warming">\n        global warming\n       </a>\n       , but the warming climate does influence certain attributes of storms. Studies in this regard show that storms tend to intensify more rapidly prior to landfall.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Wapo_Aug27_178-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Wapo_Aug27-178">\n         [176]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Weather events are due to multiple factors, and so cannot be said to be caused by one precondition, but climate change affects aspects of extreme events, and very likely worsened some of the impacts of Harvey.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-PIK_Research_Portal_31_Aug_179-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-PIK_Research_Portal_31_Aug-179">\n         [177]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In a briefing, the\n       <a href="/wiki/World_Meteorological_Organization" title="World Meteorological Organization">\n        World Meteorological Organization\n       </a>\n       stated that the quantity of rainfall from Harvey had very likely been increased by climate change. The relationship between climate change and the frequency of hurricanes (or tropical cyclones) is still unclear, and is the subject of continuing research.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Miles_Aug_29_2017_180-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Miles_Aug_29_2017-180">\n         [178]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Harvey approached Houston over sea-surface waters which were significantly above average temperatures. Warm waters provide the main source of energy for hurricanes, and increased ocean heat can result in storms being larger, more intense and longer lasting, in particular bringing greatly increased rainfall.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Atlantic2717_181-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Atlantic2717-181">\n         [179]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Wapo_Aug27_178-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Wapo_Aug27-178">\n         [176]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Sea_level_rise" title="Sea level rise">\n        Sea level rise\n       </a>\n       added to the resulting problems.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-PIK_Research_Portal_31_Aug_179-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-PIK_Research_Portal_31_Aug-179">\n         [177]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       According to officials from the Harris County Flood Control District, Harvey caused the third \'500-year\' flood in three years.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Wapo30Aug3rd500Event_182-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Wapo30Aug3rd500Event-182">\n         [180]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-183">\n        <a href="#cite_note-183">\n         [181]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-184">\n        <a href="#cite_note-184">\n         [182]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Climate_Assessment" title="National Climate Assessment">\n        National Climate Assessment\n       </a>\n       states:\n      </p>\n      <blockquote class="templatequote">\n       <p>\n        The recent increases in activity are linked, in part, to higher sea surface temperatures in the region that Atlantic hurricanes form in and move through. Numerous factors have been shown to influence these local sea surface temperatures, including natural variability, human-induced emissions of heat-trapping gases, and particulate pollution. Quantifying the relative contributions of natural and human-caused factors is an active focus of research.\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-185">\n         <a href="#cite_note-185">\n          [183]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </p>\n      </blockquote>\n      <p>\n       Warmer air can hold more water vapour, in accordance with the\n       <a href="/wiki/Clausius%E2%80%93Clapeyron_relation" title="Clausius\xe2\x80\x93Clapeyron relation">\n        Clausius\xe2\x80\x93Clapeyron relation\n       </a>\n       , and there has been a global increase of daily rainfall records.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-PIK_Research_Portal_31_Aug_179-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-PIK_Research_Portal_31_Aug-179">\n         [177]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Regional\n       <a href="/wiki/Sea_surface_temperature" title="Sea surface temperature">\n        sea surface temperatures\n       </a>\n       around Houston have risen around 0.5\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C (0.9\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F) in recent decades, which caused a 3\xe2\x80\x935% increase in moisture in the atmosphere. This had the effect of allowing Harvey to strengthen more than expected.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Mann2817_177-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Mann2817-177">\n         [175]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The water temperature of the Gulf of Mexico was above average for this time of the year, and likely to be a factor in Harvey\'s impact.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-186">\n        <a href="#cite_note-186">\n         [184]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Within a week of Harvey\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Irma" title="Hurricane Irma">\n        Hurricane Irma\n       </a>\n       formed due to the same unusually warm sea-water. Some scientists fear this may be becoming a \'new normal\'. Also higher sea-water temperatures can make hurricanes more devastating.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-187">\n        <a href="#cite_note-187">\n         [185]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The slow movement of Harvey over Texas allowed the storm to drop prolonged heavy rains on the state, as has also happened with earlier storms.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NPR.org_28_8_2017_170-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NPR.org_28_8_2017-170">\n         [168]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Harvey\'s stalled position was due to weak prevailing winds linked to a greatly expanded subtropical high pressure system over much of the US at the time, which had pushed the jet stream to the north. Research and model simulations have indicated an association between this pattern and human-caused climate change.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Mann2817_177-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Mann2817-177">\n         [175]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Mann_Rahmstorf_Kornhuber_Steinman_p.3D45242_188-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Mann_Rahmstorf_Kornhuber_Steinman_p.3D45242-188">\n         [186]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">\n        See also\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Harvey&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: See also">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <table class="mbox-small plainlinks sistersitebox" role="presentation" style="background-color:#f9f9f9;border:1px solid #aaa;color:#000">\n       <tr>\n   <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Maria" title="Hurricane Maria">\n         Hurricane Maria\n        </a>\n        \xe2\x80\x93 Another major hurricane in the 2017 Atlantic hurricane season, which devastated\n        <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico" title="Puerto Rico">\n         Puerto Rico\n        </a>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <p>\n       Other tropical cyclones that made landfall in the same region of the Texas Gulf coast:\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/1886_Indianola_hurricane" title="1886 Indianola hurricane">\n         1886 Indianola hurricane\n        </a>\n        \xe2\x80\x93 Destroyed the burgeoning port city of Indianola\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/1900_Galveston_hurricane" title="1900 Galveston hurricane">\n         1900 Galveston hurricane\n        </a>\n        \xe2\x80\x93 Deadliest natural disaster in US history, impacting Galveston with unmitigated storm surge and killing as many as 12,000\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/1932_Freeport_hurricane" title="1932 Freeport hurricane">\n         1932 Freeport hurricane\n        </a>\n        \xe2\x80\x93 Rapidly intensifying Category\xc2\xa04 hurricane that brought heavy rainfall to the Angleton and Freeport areas\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Celia" title="Hurricane Celia">\n         Hurricane Celia\n        </a>\n        (1970)\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 Produced destructive winds in the Corpus Christi area\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <div aria-label="Portals" class="noprint href="/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Harvey&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Notes">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="reflist" style="list-style-type: decimal;">\n       <div class="mw-references-wrap">\n        <ol class="references">\n         <li id="cite_note-1">\n          <span class="mw-cite-backlink">\n           <b>\n            <a href="#cite_ref-1">\n             ^\n            </a>\n           </b>\n          </span>\n          <span class="reference-text">\n           A major hurricane is a hurricane that ranks as Category\xc2\xa03 or higher on the\n           <a href="/wiki/Saffir%E2%80%93Simpson_scale" title="Saffir\xe2\x80\x93Simpson scale">\n            Saffir\xe2\x80\x93Simpson scale\n           </a>\n           .\n          </span>\n         </li>\n         <li id="cite_note-123">\n          <span class="mw-cite-backlink">\n           <b>\n            <a href="#cite_ref-123">\n             ^\n            </a>\n           </b>\n          </span>\n          <span class="reference-text">\n           All damage figures in this table are in the\n           <a href="/wiki/United_States_dollar" title="United States dollar">\n            USD\n           </a>\n           amounts of their respective year.\n          </span>\n         </li>\n        </ol>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="References">\n        References\n       </span>\n
